Song Zheyuan Goes to Baoding to Attend Hebei Province Security Meeting and Inspect the 29th Army Troops Stationed There. Song Says His Trip to Jinan with Matsumuro Has No Special Mission

(Beiping) Song Zheyuan left Beiping this afternoon for Baoding, accompanied by Deng Zhexi, Director of the Military Law Department of the Pacification Headquarters, and Song Meicun, Director of the Staff Department. Song said that his trip to Baoding was to attend the closing ceremony of the security meeting convened by the Hebei Provincial Security Department, where he would give a special speech and take the opportunity to inspect the 29th Army troops stationed there. After staying in Baoding for a short time, he would go to the Hejian area to investigate the administration of various counties. He had not met with Nishida since he arrived in Beiping, and Wang Kemin's arrival in the north was not yet certain. There had been no recent diplomatic activities in North China, and Matsumuro's trip to Jinan was probably without any special mission. The construction plan for the Cangshi Road was under study and had been submitted to the Economic and Transportation Committees to draft a plan. (4th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Song Zheyuan said that his trip to Baoding had three missions: (1) The Hebei Provincial Security Department had convened local personnel to hold a defense meeting, and the 4th was the last day, so he was going to give a speech and provide instructions on everything; (2) to inspect the troops stationed in Baoding; (3) if time permitted, after finishing the matters in Baoding, he planned to go to Hejian and other counties to inspect the highways and conduct on-site investigations into the hardships of the people to provide relief. The date of his return to Beiping was undecided. He had not yet met with Nishida since he came to Beiping. Matsumuro's trip to Jinan was certain, but the mission was unclear. Wang Kemin had recently expressed pessimism in his letters, but he had sent a letter urging him to come. Whether he would come to Beiping immediately was still uncertain, but he very much hoped he would come to Beiping. The diplomatic negotiations for Hebei and Chahar had now been suspended. He believed that diplomatic matters should be the responsibility of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and diplomatic issues should be handled directly with the Ministry. The construction of the Cangshi Road was being studied by the Economic and Transportation Committees, and a concrete plan would soon be drafted. Song concluded by saying that China could not recover without revitalizing its spirit. Although the situation was difficult, it could not rely on others to seek national salvation. Therefore, he had always advocated leading by example and safeguarding national sovereignty. (4th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Beiping) Song Zheyuan hosted a banquet for the presidents of various universities at the Diplomatic Building this afternoon, attended by Jiang Menglin, Li Rong, Xu Songming, and others. Liu Zhe, Qin Dechun, and others were invited to accompany them. During the banquet, Song explained the matters related to the upcoming examination for university graduates. (4th Dispatch)

(Baoding) The third day of the Hebei Security Conference was held as scheduled at 7:00 AM on the 4th, continuing to discuss the proposals from various counties. Committee Chairman Song left Beiping at 2:30 PM and was expected to arrive at 6:00 PM. (4th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Baoding) The General Assembly of the Security Conference announced the situation of the morning meeting on the 4th, stating that the Security Conference continued to be held at 7:00 AM on the 4th. It was heard that a detailed discussion was held on the matter of eliminating and preventing communists. With a strict method of investigation, the communists in Hebei could be expected to be eradicated in the future. (4th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Qi Xieyuan had not yet confirmed his position as a member of the Hebei-Chahar Committee. Song Zheyuan ordered Zhang Zizhong to urge him nearby, and he would go to Beiping with him in the next few days to talk with Song again to confirm the matter. (4th Dispatch)

(Beiping) The Political Council hired Qi Xieyuan as a member of the council, and the letter of appointment was delivered today. (4th Dispatch)

A Violent Earthquake Occurs in Tianshui

(Lanzhou) A violent earthquake occurred in Tianshui around 1:00 PM on the 1st, with ten consecutive aftershocks of varying sizes. Many houses and walls collapsed. (4th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Bandits with Neat Firearms Discovered in Malanyu

(Tianjin) More than 300 bandits with neat firearms were discovered in Malanyu, looting gold mines and burning and looting Moshizhuang outside the pass. The militia security teams of Zunhua, Qian'an, and Ji County were dispatched to suppress them. (4th Dispatch)

Yin Rugeng Flies Back to Tongzhou

(Tianjin) Yin Rugeng finished his business in Tianjin and flew back to Tongzhou at 9:00 AM on the 4th. (4th Dispatch)

Reorganization of the New Sui Automobile Company

(Tianjin) The business of the New Sui Automobile Company was sluggish. It was reorganized this month, and the freight for goods transported from the interior was reduced by 60%. The company also earnestly requested the four provinces of Xinjiang, Gansu, Ningxia, and Suiyuan to reduce taxes. (4th Dispatch)

Cixian Coal Mine to Start Work Soon

(Baoding) The Cixian Coal Mine was allocated 75,000 yuan from the Jingxing mines, and machines from Lincheng and Jingxing were borrowed to first open a vertical shaft. With the approval of Song Zheyuan, preparations were now complete and work could start soon. After the Lincheng mine was flooded, there were plans to allocate 50,000 yuan from the Jingxing mine to first open a small kiln. (4th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Standing Committee Meeting of the Judicial Yuan Suspended

(Nanjing) The Standing Committee meeting of the Judicial Yuan on the 4th was suspended because the President of the Yuan, Ju Zheng, and the Secretary-General, Xie Guansheng, had gone to Lushan for official business and had not returned. (4th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Chu Minyi Issues a Statement

(Nanjing) Central Committee member Chu Minyi arrived in Nanjing and spoke about the following: (1) With the persuasion of various parties, the issues between Li Zongren and Bai Chongxi in Guangxi could be resolved peacefully through political means; (2) The Chairman was still in Czechoslovakia, and a recent telegram stated that his health had not yet fully recovered, and the date of his return to the country was not yet determined; (3) The construction of the temporary venue for the National Assembly was underway and would be completed in October. The construction of the Fine Arts Exhibition Hall would be completed by the end of this month. Whether the General Election Affairs Office of the National Assembly would be moved there for office work would depend on the needs and my decision. (4th Dispatch)

Establishment Meeting of the Vegetable Oil Factory Scheduled to Open in Lushan

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Industry was preparing to establish a vegetable oil factory and had finalized the fundraising method. The shares from Sichuan, Hubei, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and the Ministry of Industry had all been paid up. The factory was scheduled to open its establishment meeting in Lushan on the 15th. Wu Dingchang, Yang Yongtai, and Lu Zuofu would all attend to elect a manager. The general office of the factory would be located in Hankou. (4th Dispatch)

Candidates for General Manager of the Agricultural Credit Bureau Still Undecided

(Nanjing) The directors and supervisors of both the government and commercial sectors of the Agricultural Credit Bureau of the Ministry of Industry had been nominated. The general bureau was to be located in Nanjing, and Qian Xinzhi was nominated as the general manager, but Qian was inconvenient to reside in Nanjing permanently and was declining the position. If Qian agreed to take the position, then Zou Bingwen would be appointed as the deputy general manager. (4th Dispatch)

Further Research Needed on Starting Inheritance Tax

(Nanjing) The general issues of starting inheritance tax had been discussed by the Legal and Financial Special Committees of the Central Political Council, and the results had been achieved. However, regarding the inheritance tax system, there were those who advocated adopting the gross inheritance tax system and those who advocated adopting the combination inheritance tax system (i.e., the so-called inheritance tax). Which theory was more appropriate had become the central issue of review and still required careful research before a decision could be made. (4th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Military Purges, Changes, and Coups D'état (III)

— Jia He

Past history told Ugaki that to realize his long-cherished wish of many years, he had to remove the obstacles blocking his progress, that is, he had to purge the Araki faction. Minister of the Army Terauchi, bearing the public's expectation of cleaning up the "February 26th Incident," bravely placed the four great generals, Araki, Mazaki, Honjo, and Kawashima, into the reserve, and used the ordinance restricting the Minister of the Army to active-duty generals, cutting off any possibility of the aforementioned four great generals from making a comeback. Thereafter, every time he issued a list of changes, it made the Zaibatsu applaud: (1) The changes on March 23rd used the name of "bearing responsibility for the coup d'état" to insert his comrade, Kozo Kanro, as Vice Minister of the Army, giving the position to Umezu Mijiro, temporarily taking a backseat at the Aviation Headquarters. General Sugiyama Hajime avoided being the target of attacks and was transferred to the General Staff Headquarters, allowing the Chief of Staff, Nishio Juyo (Chief of Staff of the Kwantung Army) from the central faction, to take the position. As for the officers who participated in the coup d'état, such as Major General Sato Shozaburo, they were all "placed on standby" (i.e., dismissed). The only one from the Araki faction who could be called proud that day was Okamura Yasuji, who was transferred from the Second Department Chief of the General Staff Headquarters to the Second Division Commander. (2) The changes on March 28th completed the unfinished work of the previous decision. He dismissed the direct superiors of the participating troops, such as the commander of the 1st Infantry Regiment, Colonel Koto Megumu, the commander of the 3rd Infantry Regiment, Colonel Shibuya Saburo, and the commander of the 3rd Guards Infantry Regiment, Colonel Sonoyama Mitsuzo, and other officers, a total of eleven people. The other 120 personnel who were changed were also lieutenant-colonel and below. (3) The changes on July 10th placed all the aforementioned personnel on standby into the reserve. Lieutenant General Komine Kohei (dismissed on April 2nd), the Tokyo garrison commander during the coup d'état, also suffered the same fate. Although there were Hashimoto Toranosuke (former commander of the Guards Division) and Hori Takeo (former commander of the 1st Division), who were close to Army Minister Hayashi, as foils, the Araki faction's strongholds, the 1st and 2nd Guards Divisions, were almost eradicated.

At the same time, the news that "the scope of the August changes is quite large" appeared in the newspapers. As expected, the number of people transferred, reassigned, and dismissed reached more than 3,000. Among them, the most important was Sugiyama Hajime, the main character in Army Minister Hayashi's military purge mentioned earlier. In addition to being appointed as a military councillor, he also replaced Nishi Yoshiichi (placed in the reserve) and was promoted to Director-General of Military Education, one of the three chiefs of the army. Although Lieutenant General Kishimoto Ayato advanced to the rank of general one step ahead of him (but was dismissed at the same time), every commentator predicted the date of Sugiyama's promotion to general. As a result, Lieutenant General Kozo Kanro, who had been slightly suppressed for a time, was transferred to the Director-General of the Army Aviation Headquarters, and Hata Shunroku, the former head of the Aviation Headquarters, was transferred to the commander of the Taiwan Army. Imai Kiyotake, who had been active on the personnel stage after his predecessor Nagata, was appointed as the commander of the 4th Division. The above people celebrating their promotion were all seen as people of the Ugaki system or quasi-Ugaki system. From this, we know that the central stage of the Japanese army today is mostly dominated by Ugaki.

On the other hand, let's look at Araki's lineup! Imai Kiyotake's position as commander of the 4th Division was originally for Tatekawa Yoshitsugu. Lieutenant General Tatekawa, like the president of the Veterans Association, General Suzuki Sojuro, was a senior cavalry officer and son-in-law of Major General Morioka Masayuki. After the Manchurian Incident, he gave speeches with Araki in resonance. It was unsuitable to have such a person stationed in Japan's "economic heart," the capital of the Kansai Zaibatsu, Osaka, everyone knew this. Now he and Lieutenant General Obata Toshishiro were placed in the reserve at the same time. Another person we want to talk about is the commander of the Taiwan Army, Yanagawa Heisuke. His friendship with Araki can be proven by the small matter of his eldest daughter Kazuko's marriage, which troubled the general and baron. Of course, private feelings are one thing, and public affairs are another. The two should not be confused, but Araki's favorite theorist, Date Ryujo, listed Lieutenant General Yanagawa as a member of Araki's camp. At a time when the southward advance was being loudly chanted, he was recalled to the central government (appointed to the General Staff Headquarters). This can explain to us that the work of "military purification" has reached from the central government to the colonies. If the "military purification" of the colonies is the most difficult, then Yanagawa's transfer can be regarded as the first signal, which is also unknown.

Studying the organization and power of the Japanese military is very interesting. In a country with such consolidated central authority, power is in the hands of the central government? There is no problem. However, the garrisons in places like Osaka and the colonies of Manchuria and Taiwan also occupy important positions. Some are recalled to the central government from the local area, increasing their power, and some are transferred out from the central government, weakening their power. We can use the familiar former Shanghai military attache, Lieutenant Colonel Kagesa Teiaki, as our illustration. On the day of his honorable transfer, he promoted the policies of the young and strong faction in the department with the qualification of "Manchuria-Mongolia class leader," but now he is transferred to the artillery 2nd regiment stationed in Sendai, giving us a feeling of promotion in name but demotion in fact.

According to the above facts, the work of "military purification" has indeed come to a fairly satisfactory end. What about "the overall renewal of governance"? The facilities of the Hirota Cabinet gave people great disappointment. Therefore, Army Minister Terauchi publicly declared on June 2nd: "The purification of the military department is closely related to the general renewal of governance and cannot be separated." (Yomiuri, 3rd), which was tantamount to a blow to Hirota. Early on July 26th, he (General Terauchi) went west to visit the Ise Grand Shrine and frankly expressed his dissatisfaction with the current cabinet to the press, saying with the qualification of "Minister of State": "The overall renewal of governance is the demand of the times. Ministers who cannot implement it should resign without hesitation, leaving behind ministers with vigor. As for myself, perhaps I belong to the weak, which is also unknown." (Daima). Was this hinting at using resignation to overthrow the cabinet? When he arrived in Nagoya in the afternoon, he replied, "I won't resign so easily" (ibid).

Page 7

The United States and the Philippines. Certain Island to be a Permanent Naval Base for the U.S.

Washington, D.C. U.S. High Commissioner to the Philippines, Murphy, gave a speech here today, stating that the people of the Philippines are politically ready for independence, but economically, maintaining its stability is a serious practical problem. Mr. Murphy said that the Filipinos have sufficient legislative capacity, and praised President Quezon, the Chief Justice of the Supreme Court, and other government officials for their competence and integrity, so he has great hope for the future of the Philippines. The people of the Philippines now need guidance and support, so they must remain under the jurisdiction of the United States for at least ten more years. (3rd National Telegram)

(Tokyo) According to the report from Consul General Uchiyama in Manila received by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 4th, the Palawan Provincial Council of the Philippine Federation recently passed a resolution to request President Quezon to propose to the U.S. government that part or all of the province become an important base for the U.S. Navy and permanently belong to the U.S. The province is located in the South China Sea and is a military stronghold facing the Sulu Sea, with a total area of 4,500 square miles. It used to be a colony and fishing ground for American prisoners and occupies an excellent position. According to this resolution, it is hoped that the exception clause for naval bases in the Philippine Independence Act will be applied. Therefore, the voluntary abandonment of independence by the military stronghold of Palawan Island and its subjugation under the rule of the U.S. government is quite noteworthy from various points of view. (4th Allied Dispatch)

(Washington) People here are discussing today that the recent cracking of two Japanese spy cases will have a considerable impact politically and diplomatically. Some military experts in the army and navy believe that the impact of the Thompson case and the Forbes case can be summarized as follows: (1) Warning other spies not to sell U.S. military secrets to foreign governments; (2) Indirectly warning Japan, meaning that the United States is capable of cracking down on spy cases that are more serious than these two cases. It is said that Thompson impersonated a navy man, and Forbes had been out of the navy for a long time, so neither of them could provide valuable information to foreign countries. (3rd National Telegram)

British Labour Party Leader Travels to Soviet Russia

(London) Major Attlee, leader of the opposition Labour Party in Parliament, is scheduled to depart for the Soviet Union tomorrow. He claims that the trip is purely for travel, but he will also take the opportunity to study the general situation in the Soviet Union. (3rd Havas Dispatch)

Two German Warships Cover Spanish Rebels, German Military Officers Visit Rebel Leaders, British and French Officials Quite Surprised

(London) Officials here are quite surprised by the actions of the German pocket battleship Deutschland. The ship sailed to the port of Ceuta in Morocco, just as two Spanish government warships were engaged in battle with rebel batteries on the shore, making it impossible for them to effectively bombard the shore. News was also received that the officers of the Deutschland had been formally received by General Franco, the leader of the rebels, increasing the officials' concern. (4th Reuters Dispatch)

(Paris) The German 10,000-ton cruiser Deutschland and the destroyer Luchs arrived at the port of Ceuta in Spanish Morocco yesterday morning. All the officers of the warships went ashore to visit General Franco, the commander-in-chief of the Spanish rebels. Responsible sources stated that the anchoring of German warships in the port of Ceuta was a common occurrence under the current system in Morocco and was not a recurrence of the Agadir Incident today (Editor's note: In 1910, Germany sent the cruiser Panther to the port of Agadir in Morocco to demonstrate to France. France and Germany subsequently concluded an agreement in 1911 to resolve the Moroccan question). However, the fact that the German warship commanders visited the Spanish rebel leaders showed that Germany, even if it did not directly interfere in Spanish internal affairs, at least publicly expressed sympathy for the rebels. This move was particularly unsettling. Whether the motive for the visit was to discuss the repatriation of German refugees or due to international courtesy was currently unknown. Since no countries have recognized the rebel leaders, the so-called "courtesy" must also have a special meaning. (4th Havas Agency Dispatch)

Tangier, Morocco Special dispatch from our correspondent Regarding the German warship's arrival at the port of Ceuta, the Spanish rebels had received the news several days before. According to a key figure in diplomatic circles, "The visit of the German warship commander to the rebel leader, General Franco, is the most serious matter. Although those around Franco say that this move was only a courtesy exchange, in reality, the conversation lasted for more than an hour, and the rebels also clearly regarded this action of the German warship as an expression of sympathy for them." Also, when the rebel officers accompanied the German warship officers to tour the port of Ceuta this morning, they were all smug and showed it on their faces, which is also noteworthy. (4th Havas Agency Dispatch)

Ceuta, Morocco The German 10,000-ton pocket battleship Deutschland and the German destroyer Luchs entered the port here this morning and were warmly welcomed. All the ships in the port fired salutes to pay their respects. General Franco, the leader of the Spanish rebels, received the German officers in the old palace. It was heard that the German warships came to protect German expatriates. (3rd Reuters Dispatch)

(London) The British government sent a reply to the French ambassador this afternoon regarding the French government's request for the UK, France, Italy, and other countries to issue a joint statement of non-interference in the Spanish civil unrest. (4th Reuters Dispatch)

(Rome) After French Ambassador Chamberlain met with Foreign Minister Ciano yesterday regarding the issue of non-interference in the Spanish civil unrest, the Propaganda Department issued a press release stating, "Foreign Minister Ciano has taken note of the oral note submitted by Ambassador Chamberlain, but a reply can only be given after consulting with the Prime Minister (currently on summer vacation at a villa in the Romana province)." (4th Havas Dispatch)

(Berlin) French Ambassador Ponsot met with Foreign Minister Neurath this morning regarding the issue of non-interference in the Spanish civil unrest. According to semi-official sources, Germany is willing to engage in consultations with the countries concerned to establish a "non-interference" agreement, but only if Soviet Russia also does not interfere in the Spanish civil unrest. (4th Havas Dispatch)

120,000 People in Soviet Russia Hold a Meeting to Support Spain, Telegram to the Spanish Government, Workers Donate Half a Month's Wages

(Moscow) On August 2nd and 3rd, enterprises and institutions in Moscow and Leningrad held meetings one after another to sympathize with the Spanish people's defense of democratic freedom and resistance to the rebellion of reactionary soldiers. Resolutions were passed everywhere to raise funds and aid the soldiers defending the Spanish Republic. On August 3rd, the trade union convened a general meeting in Red Square, attended by 120,000 people. Shirvernik, the secretary of the Federal Labor Union, workers from various Moscow factories, writer Fadeev, and researcher Fersman successively gave speeches. The conference unanimously passed a telegram to congratulate Spanish President Azaña and Prime Minister Giral. (4th TASS Dispatch)

(Moscow) Members of the Moscow Trade Union are willing to donate half of their monthly wages to support the defense of Spanish civil governance. (3rd Reuters Dispatch)

The Truth About French Aircraft Participating: Belgium Manages Arms Exports

(Paris) According to the right-wing Bai Ribao, France recently dispatched four aircraft to Spain to transport French expatriates out of the country to avoid danger. Unexpectedly, after the aircraft arrived in Spain, they were requisitioned by the Spanish government for military use. In addition, the orthodox socialist People's Daily and the communist Humanity reported that the famous French stunt pilot Detroyat was recruiting pilots to go to Spain to collaborate in combat under the command of rebel leader General Franco. (4th Havas Dispatch)

Brussels The Cabinet recently organized a committee dedicated to handling arms trade issues. The committee recently received a report stating that both the Spanish government forces and the rebels were being provided with arms by foreign countries. It held a meeting at 3:00 PM today and immediately decided that all arms factories in the country must obtain a license before exporting arms. This measure should be revoked only after all national arms factories are nationalized in accordance with the cabinet's declaration of general policy. (3rd Havas Dispatch)

Spanish Expatriate Protection Issue: UK and U.S. Policies are the Same, Expatriate Evacuation Reaches a Conclusion, Those Unwilling to Leave Risk Their Own Dangers

(Washington) Secretary of State Hull warned American expatriates residing in Spain today that the U.S. government could neither guarantee that Spain could maintain the status quo for a long time, nor could it determine that American ships could contact American expatriates at any time to transport them out of the country. The government had advised all American diplomatic personnel to immediately leave their families outside of Spain. The U.S. warship Quincy reported that it had departed for Malaga and stated that traffic between Barcelona and Malaga had been disrupted. (3rd National Telegram)

(London) The Admiralty announced today that all British expatriates who wished to leave Spain have now been evacuated. Several British warships may withdraw from the Spanish coast. British people still residing in Spain have been notified that they will be responsible for their own risks from now on. (4th Reuters Dispatch)

Gibraltar The strength of the British fleet stationed here has increased since the arrival of the 31,000-ton battleship Queen Elizabeth. (4th Reuters Dispatch)

(London) The battleship Queen Elizabeth (31,000 tons) is scheduled to leave the port of Gibraltar today and sail to Valencia, Alicante, Barcelona, ​​and other places in eastern Spain to transport expatriates back to the country. The armored cruiser Devonshire (10,000 tons) here has also been ordered to sail to Malta Island, and then return to its home country from there. The ship has already left Spain with 468 refugees, including the Norwegian and Venezuelan ambassadors to Spain. According to news from Valencia, Spain, the city has now returned to quiet, as have Barcelona, ​​Vichy, Coruña, and Ferrol. (4th Havas Dispatch)

(Washington) Wendelin, the third secretary of the U.S. Embassy in Spain, reported to the State Department today that there were still 46 American expatriates, 16 Puerto Ricans, and 11 Filipinos in the embassy, and 75 American expatriates, 25 Puerto Ricans, and 19 Filipinos outside the embassy. When the rebellion first started, there were many American expatriates here, but most of them have now left the country. (3rd National Telegram)

Leftist Figures from Various Countries Form Volunteer Army to Join the War; Fierce Fighting Across Spain

Madrid - Fierce fighting continues across Spain between government troops and rebel factions, but the true situation is unclear. The rebel offensive against Madrid is in an unfavorable position. Although they maintain their position on the Guadalajara front line in the nearby mountains, it is evident that they are experiencing a shortage of supplies. After strong reinforcements from the government arrived from Valencia, they are about to advance on the rebels in the area. According to sources in Barcelona, more than two hundred leftist figures from various countries have formed a volunteer army, arrived from France, and offered their services to the government. Yesterday, sixteen government aircraft carried out a large-scale bombing of Zaragoza and key points on the Aragon front line, encircling and routing the rebel cavalry. It is reported that a large number of rebels have surrendered. Furthermore, according to sources in Biarritz, a French border town, two Spanish military aircraft, en route from Madrid to San Sebastian, landed here yesterday due to the pilots losing their way. The pilots have been detained by the French police. The aircraft are equipped with machine guns, carry a large quantity of ammunition, and government propaganda materials, and are currently being guarded by French forces. (Reuters, 4th)

French Border - There is heavy fighting across Spain today. The battle of Oviedo is particularly fierce. Government forces have surrounded the entire city with landmines, effectively detaining all the rebels and 60,000 residents within. If the city falls, there will likely be a terrible massacre. The rebels are attempting to retake cities such as San Sebastian and Ronda, but the government forces have control of the coast and border, making their position difficult to shake. Government aircraft bombed the northern rebel forces today. The transatlantic aviator Loda has volunteered to serve the government. It is claimed that he bombed a train of rebel supply vehicles en route from Jaraguad to Valladolid, which then caught fire, causing many rebel casualties. (National Telegram, 3rd)

Madrid - Cannon fire in the mountain passes north of Madrid has subsided slightly today, only to resume with greater intensity. A government force led by General Mengada has charged the rebel lines, intending to penetrate deep into enemy territory to allow the main force to advance. It is now reported that there is fierce hand-to-hand combat. (National Telegram, 3rd)

Spanish Rebel Headquarters - After fearlessly engaging the government forces' machine-gun positions in hand-to-hand combat, the rebels have now captured the Guadalajara mountain pass. Approximately eight hundred rebels were killed in action. After the rebel victory, their right flank has advanced to a superior position and can now link up with the central rebel forces in the Beitrage Valley, preparing to launch a new offensive. The rebels launched a surprise attack on the government forces in this battle, and by the time the government forces realized what was happening and returned fire, it was too late. Although hundreds of rebels were seriously injured and fell to the ground, the remaining troops continued to surge forward, engaging in hand-to-hand combat, which was resolved in a matter of minutes. The rebels captured fifty government soldiers. The number of government casualties is unknown. General De, a former adjutant to the deposed King Alfonso, arrived here today to take command of the rebel forces here. (National Telegram, 3rd)

Spanish Burgos - (This city is the location of the Spanish Revolutionary Army's "National Defense Government." Our correspondent arrived here yesterday from Hendaye, France, to inspect the situation. Along the way through the province of Navarre, everything was very quiet. Upon arriving here, we immediately visited General Mola, the commander of the Revolutionary Army's Northern Front. According to his declaration, he is very confident about the future of the war. Furthermore, according to sources in Seville, General Del Llano, the commander of the Andalusian Division in the city, and the commander of the Revolutionary Army's Southern Front, announced last night in a radio broadcast that a government force departing from Ciudad Real province had been defeated by the Revolutionary Army, with 200 government soldiers killed. In addition, according to sources in Zaragoza, the Revolutionary Army has repelled the People's Front militia.) (Havas, 4th)

Madrid - A special dispatch from our war correspondent states that fierce fighting broke out yesterday in the Somo Sierra mountain pass north of the capital (70 kilometers from Madrid). At 5:00 AM at dawn, the rebels suddenly burst out of the mountain pass with great momentum. The government forces, composed of the militia led by General Galan, bore the brunt of the attack and immediately ordered a counterattack, which quickly turned into hand-to-hand combat. The clash of blades and the sight of blood and flesh flying everywhere made this battle the most intense since the outbreak of hostilities. By evening, General Liguera, the commander of the Aragon front, directed the government forces in the battle. The two sides fought fiercely all day until nightfall, when they ceased fighting. The rebels were defeated and retreated, suffering more than 300 casualties, with many deserting. The government forces also suffered more than 80 casualties, but reinforcements arrived continuously. After the government forces won the victory, they consolidated their positions at night to prepare for continued fighting. In addition, a decisive battle is expected to break out in the Leon mountain pass within the next three or four days. (Havas, 4th)

Tangier - A special dispatch from our correspondent states that two Spanish government battleships, the "Jaime I" and the "Libertad," recently opened fire on the Spanish-controlled port of Ceuta on the northern shore of the Strait of Gibraltar. Our reporter happened to be aboard the Spanish merchant ship "Comete Lusa," en route from Tangier to British Gibraltar, and witnessed the battle. The shells fired by the two ships landed in Ceuta and the rebel barracks. After fifteen minutes, five rebel aircraft flew out of the port of Terifa and soared into the sky, dropping bombs on the two ships. The two ships also opened fire with anti-aircraft guns in retaliation, but the aircraft were flying very high, and the shells failed to hit. While the two sides were engaged in fierce fighting, the residents of Ceuta were extremely alarmed, and some had already fled to Algeciras. (Havas, 3rd)

Bayonne, France - According to sources in Gijón, northern Spain, the Spanish cruiser "Almirante Cervera," after defecting to the rebels, bombarded the city yesterday, causing many casualties among the residents. The city authorities immediately warned the rebel ship via radio that if it continued to bombard the city, they would execute all 2,500 rebel soldiers detained within the city. It is reported that the ship immediately ceased its bombardment after this warning was issued. (Havas, 4th)

Tangier - According to unconfirmed reports, several Spanish government and rebel aircraft engaged in aerial combat this morning near British Gibraltar. As a result, the government aircraft were victorious, and two rebel aircraft were forced to land, while two others fled back to Ceuta, Morocco. (Havas, 4th)

Spanish Government Reduces Burden on the People; Confiscates Church Property

Madrid - The government has recently issued four orders: (1) Residents' rent, for those paying less than 201 pesetas per month, will be reduced by 50%; (2) Rent arrears may be temporarily deferred; (3) All commercial promissory notes that were previously granted temporary deferment will be extended to August 9; (4) Private citizens may not withdraw more than 2,000 pesetas from banks and savings institutions each month. In addition, the government has ordered the dismissal and investigation of many officials and officers of the army and navy who have defected to the rebels, including officers of the battleship "Cala D". (Havas, 4th)

Madrid - The local militia in Asturia searched a Catholic church today and found 300,000 pesetas in government bonds hidden behind paintings. This is one scene from the nationwide confiscation of church property. (National Telegram, 3rd)

Madrid - Government forces have now dropped 13,200 pounds of bombs on Palma. Workers and mechanics here have resumed work, but automobile drivers are still on strike. The government has announced that the rebels are actively preparing for war, but the government forces' defensive positions are solid and secure. Although the rebels in the north have gained some ground, the government forces in the west are in a superior position. (National Telegram, 3rd)

Madrid - The Ministry of Interior today ordered the organization of an Automobile Transportation Committee to be responsible for requisitioning vehicles, and controlling and allocating national transportation. It also ordered the formation of volunteer units from the current militia. (National Telegram, 3rd)

Madrid - The cabinet has recently issued an order to dismiss four university professors suspected of supporting the rebellion, including former cabinet member Villanova. In addition, the government has nationalized the following three private railway companies: the Northwest Railway Company, the Aragon Central Railway Company, and the Massaya Railway Company (which operates between Madrid, Zaragoza, and Alicante). (Havas, 4th)

Concerns in Parisian Diplomatic Circles Regarding Spain; Believe Germany and Italy's Attitudes are Suspicious

(Paris) - Diplomatic circles here are very concerned about the situation in Spain. Although news came from that country last night stating that fierce fighting had broken out in the Guadalajara mountains north of the capital, the ultimate victor has yet to be determined. If this situation remains unchanged for a long time, it will inevitably have an impact internationally due to the different attitudes of various countries. This is a matter of great concern. According to diplomatic circles, the British government will likely give a satisfactory response today to France's proposal for a non-intervention agreement in the Spanish situation. On the Italian side, according to sources in Rome, Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano met with French Ambassador Chambrun yesterday. People here were quite uneasy upon hearing this news, fearing that the Italian government would not be as eager as the British and French governments to establish a neutrality agreement. In addition, Italian newspapers have not said a word about the French ambassador's request, but instead criticized France for not helping the Madrid government, and pointed to the fact that Spanish gold is being shipped into Paris as proof of French aid to that government. As for the issue of Italian aircraft flying to Spanish Morocco, the Italian public has remained silent on the matter, and government officials have consistently stated that the investigation has not yet been completed. In light of all these factors, Italy's attitude is indeed concerning. Moreover, news from Germany is even more worrying. According to a telegram from Tangier, an international neutral port, the German cruiser "Deutschland" and the destroyer "Luchs" both arrived in Ceuta, Spanish Africa, at 9:00 AM yesterday. The commanders of the two ships immediately went ashore to visit General Franco, the leader of the Spanish rebels. The attitude of Germany in this action is very suspicious. Furthermore, according to news from Moscow, the people there held a gathering yesterday to express their solidarity with the Spanish workers in their struggle against the Fascists. At the same time, the rebel radio station in Spanish Ceuta broadcast a message claiming that the Soviet Union is indeed providing assistance to the Madrid government. All of this news makes people even more fearful. At this juncture, it is imperative that major countries seek a compromise on this issue to avoid the spread of disaster. (Havas, 4th)

Therefore, another national policy cabinet meeting will be held in late August. (Domei News Agency, 4th)

Important Results of Solar Eclipse Observation by Soviet Scientists

(Moscow, TASS, July 6) - The Soviet astronomical observation team obtained 150 photographs of the solar eclipse on June 19. The Polkovo observation team obtained extremely valuable red shell spectroscopic photographs at Akbulak, which clearly show the fine structure of the red shell, allowing for a detailed understanding of the upper layers of the solar atmosphere. In the past, the red shell was thought to be a continuous structure, but it has now been proven to be composed of numerous independent parts, shaped like small rivers. Previously, due to blurry photographs, these countless small rivers appeared to merge into one. These spectroscopic photographs will shed new light on the question of the nature of the solar atmosphere.

Secondly, the photography of the solar corona was a complete success. These photographs were taken using a special lens manufactured in the Soviet Union. The photography was conducted in five locations, from the North Caucasus to the Pacific coast. Therefore, Soviet astronomers obtained a large set of films, allowing them to understand in detail the changes in the solar corona during the two hours of the solar eclipse. These photographs were taken using the same method and can be compared to reveal the internal movement of the solar corona.

The study of radio wave emissions during the solar eclipse also yielded the most important results. The materials obtained reveal that the electrical guidance of the stratosphere, which helps ground-based radio wave broadcasting, is due to the power of sunlight ultraviolet radiation.

The above is only the most important result of the solar eclipse observation. The materials obtained through precise research in the future will greatly contribute to the study of the physical structure of the solar and the Earth's stratosphere.

Travelogue of Japan (11)

— Our Correspondent Hu Zhongchi and Hu Yizang

While we were visiting the editorial department, Mr. Kamio, who was working, put down his pen and came over to greet us. He accompanied us into the editor-in-chief's office. This room was connected to a large hall, with several desks placed in the corners and a large oval table in the center, surrounded by many chairs. The executives of the Asahi Shimbun often gathered there to discuss editorial policies.

Mr. Kamio introduced us to the editor-in-chief, Mr. Harada Jozo. We sat down at the large table, eating ice fruit while talking with Mr. Harada. This kind and elderly man with thick eyebrows and a short beard inspired our respect with his earnest attitude and erudite conversation. We asked him about news editing techniques. In addition to receiving various helpful instructions, we were also honored to receive his book, "The Talk of News." Perhaps because our surname was Hu, he asked about Dr. Hu Shih of our country. We were ashamed that after so many years in the news industry, we had not yet met this master of the New Literature enlightenment era. From Harada's question, we couldn't help but think that Dr. Hu, at least in the eyes of foreigners, was still a representative of the Chinese intellectual class in the new era. Therefore, we must urge him to publish his political views more cautiously. Seeing his recent articles, it seems he has revised his original, somewhat inappropriate political thoughts, which is relatively gratifying.

While we were talking with the editor-in-chief Harada, the president of Asahi Shimbun, Ueno Seiichi, the chairman of the board, Murayama Zenkyo, and the chief editor, Kogen Misao, walked into the editor-in-chief's office through a side door. Mr. Kamio introduced us to each of them. Ueno and Murayama, the two big bosses of the Asahi Shimbun, were both wearing black suits, showing their high status. President Ueno, who is now 51 years old, looked older than his actual age because of his slightly bald head. The expression on his smiling, reddish, jujube-shaped face showed that he was not only a brilliant businessman but also an outstanding politician. Murayama and Kogen both had short beards and looked older than Ueno. We exchanged greetings with several key figures of the Asahi Kingdom. During the greetings, Murayama asked us the following questions:

"If I were to go to your country now, would your people genuinely welcome me?"

"If you were to visit our country, Mr. Murayama, our news industry would certainly welcome you sincerely. However, if you mean to test the feelings of the entire nation, it seems it is still a bit early."

"Then are you saying that such a time will never come?"

Afterwards, we asked Kamio about the history of the Asahi Shimbun. According to him, the Osaka Asahi Shimbun was founded in Meiji 12 (1889) by Murayama Ryuhei. Initially, it published only one sheet per day on a very small scale. In Meiji 14, it received financial assistance from Ueno Riichi, and under their joint management, the number of pages increased and sales also increased greatly. In Meiji 21, it acquired the Tokyo Mezame Shimbun and reorganized it as the Tokyo Asahi Shimbun. As a result, its business continued to develop, eventually reaching a circulation of over two million (combined for the Osaka and Tokyo editions). Ueno Riichi and Murayama Ryuhei were the fathers of the current president and chairman of the board. Statues of them are erected at the top of the stairs outside the editorial department. Mr. Kamio accompanied us there to pay our respects. We then bid farewell to the hosts gathered in the editor-in-chief's office and declined Mr. Kamio's banquet repeatedly, leaving the Asahi Kingdom.

Japanese Advisor to the Hebei-Chahar Political Council. The Mission of Assuming the Post of Hebei-Chahar Advisor is to Seek Happiness for the People of North China

Tianjin Correspondence: The newly hired Japanese advisor to the Hebei-Chahar Political Council, Nishida Koichi, arrived in Tianjin yesterday and will soon go to Peiping to take office. Recently, Nishida met with reporters at the Yamato Hotel in the Japanese Concession. According to him, "I accepted the invitation of the Hebei-Chahar authorities. After arriving in Tianjin, I originally intended to go to Peiping as soon as possible, but I have been delayed because the negotiations here have not been completed. I have already found a residence in Yangrou Hutong, Dongcheng, Peiping. I plan to go to Peiping alone on the 3rd. My family will stay in Tianjin temporarily. After I arrive in Peiping, I will arrange and renovate the interior of the residence. I will return to Tianjin again after staying for one day. I plan to bring my family to Peiping on the 6th, and then visit Chairman Song Zheyuan to formally take office. I came to China after the Russo-Japanese War. I first worked at the Fushun Island Coal Mine, and then came to North China. In between, I traveled around Europe and America for more than a year. After returning, I went to Peiping again to serve as a secretary at the embassy. Before two years had passed, I transferred to Jinan, and so on until now. I have been in China for a total of eight and a half years, which is only six months short of the saying 'nine years facing the wall.' My main mission in assuming the post of Hebei-Chahar advisor is to assist Chairman Song in seeking happiness for the society and people of North China, and to promote mutual assistance and mutual benefit between China and Japan. The cooperation and co-prosperity of China and Japan will certainly not only benefit China or only benefit Japan. Therefore, I am determined to strive for mutual benefit and reciprocity to seek the welfare of the people of China and Japan."

Chen Juesheng, Director of the Beining Railway Bureau, was very pleased with the arrival of the new Hebei-Chahar Political Council advisor, Nishida Koichi, who was an old friend. Yesterday afternoon at 7 p.m., he specially hosted a banquet at the Beining official residence on Haihe Road in the Special District One to welcome him. He also invited Consul General of Tianjin, Tajiri Aiyi, and Consuls Nishida and Nagai to attend. The atmosphere was very friendly and convivial. (August 2nd)

A General Overview of Chahar Province's Politics: Extremely Dire Finances, Depressed Commerce, and the Chahar North Issue is Under Negotiation

Zhangjiakou Correspondence: Since taking office, Liu Ruming, Chairman of the Chahar Provincial Government, has strived to improve the politics of Chahar Province. He has put forward four policies as the foundation for his administration: safeguarding public security, purging officialdom, strictly prohibiting the Communist bandits, and fostering friendly relations. He has been coping with everything in a difficult environment in the past month and has done a good job. However, the only difficulty in Chahar Province at present is the financial problem. The financial revenue of Chahar Province has always relied on tax revenue as the only source, with local land tax being secondary. Zhangjiakou is the throat connecting trade with Mongolia's Kulun. In previous years, the annual revenue of the Zhangduo Customs was more than one million yuan. Zhangjiakou's commerce was prosperous, and local tax revenue was also considerable. Since the Mongolian issue occurred, trade between Kulun and Zhangjiakou has ceased. Not only has tax revenue been cut off, but Zhangjiakou's commerce has also been greatly affected. In addition, the six counties of Chahar North have successively been abandoned, reducing land tax revenue by one-third. The total annual land tax of the sixteen counties of Chahar Province is more than three million yuan. It is now estimated that this year's revenue will be less than two million yuan, and the indirect huge losses are not included. When Liu Ruming took office as chairman, it was after the upper and lower levels had been busy with collection, and there was no land tax revenue. Moreover, the financial deficit was more than 300,000 yuan, and the situation was difficult to cope with. Therefore, there is almost no financial budget in Chahar Province at present. He only adopts austerity policies and strives to reduce expenditures. He is working hard to support himself without any other way. However, he is still striving to do what he can for local construction. The new construction of the Dayang River Xuanyang Bridge cost more than 30,000 yuan. He is also striving to improve education funding. This year, he also increased education funding by 4,000 yuan for the purpose of adding high school classes. The garrison in Chahar Province, in addition to the 143rd Division of Liu, which is directly under the 29th Army and whose military pay is allocated by the central government, there is also the Security Office, with monthly expenses of more than 30,000 yuan, and four local military brigades, with monthly expenses of 130,000 to 140,000 yuan. The two items total 170,000 yuan, all of which rely on local revenue to maintain.

After the six counties of Chahar North outside the pass, Zhangbei, Guyuan, Kangbao, Baochang, Shangdu, and Duolun, and the three administrative bureaus of Chongli, Shangyi, and Huade were abandoned, news was cut off, and very few outsiders knew the whole truth. The traffic between Zhangyuan and the six counties of Chahar North is now only operated by four Japanese-owned automobile companies: Wenlin, Donglu, Zhangduo, and Dabeit, The vehicles that travel back and forth are very strictly inspected and, other than merchants, it is difficult for other people to pass through. According to news obtained here, the Mongolian puppet government, which claims to have three armies, is actually no more than 10,000 people. Li Shouxin is the puppet Minister of Military and Political Affairs, with 2,000 troops under his command. Wang Daoyi serves as the border defense commander, also with about 1,000 troops. It is heard that Zhao Kuige, Wang Zixiu, and other miscellaneous soldiers from Shandong are all serving in Wang's troops. It is heard that the Mongolian puppet government is located in Jiabusi Temple and is expanding its forces, organizing airplane teams, machine gun teams, and tank teams, so the future is not optimistic.

After the abandonment of the six counties of Chahar North, a few miles outside Dajingmen in Zhangjiakou is someone else's sphere of influence. Fortunately, the market in Zhangjiakou is as peaceful as usual, and the people are still living in peace. Every day, Taiping Park, Forest Park, Zhongshan Park, and other places are crowded with tourists, but the market commerce is unusually depressed due to the influence of the current situation. According to the Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, Wang Daoxiu, and the Standing Committee Member, Wang Guitang, there are 3,300 businesses in Zhangyuan. 2,300 to 400 have joined the Chamber of Commerce, and more than 1,000 have not. The main commodities are fur and grain. In the past, when Chahar Province and Mongolia's Kulun had normal trade relations, Zhangjiakou's trade volume was more than 50 million yuan. Now, business has plummeted and is less than 30 million yuan. Moreover, eight or nine out of ten merchants have suffered losses, and they are crying out in pain. Some cannot help but feel sad about the past and present. The population of Zhangjiakou is over 100,000. The number of Japanese residents is increasing daily, reaching 300. The number of Russian residents is decreasing, and there are only 40 to 50 left. Both Japan and Russia have consulates in Zhangjiakou, and the Japanese military also has a special agency in Zhangjiakou. Mongolians also often travel between Mongolia and Zhangyuan. In addition, a part of Manchus live in Zhangyuan's Shangdongying and Xiadongying.

Liu Ruming, Chairman of the Chahar Provincial Government, was previously ordered by the central government to concurrently serve as a member of the Hebei-Chahar Political Council. He specially went from Zhangjiakou to Peiping to take office, attended the regular meetings of the Political Council, and met with Chairman Song Zheyuan to report on the political situation in Chahar Province and ask for instructions. He has now completed his official duties and took the private carriage attached to the Pingsui Railway 303rd train from Peiping to Baotou on July 31 to return to Chahar. He arrived in Zhangyuan at 0:05 early on the 1st of this month. (1st)

Under Japanese Control, Actively Developing Rehe's Industry. Abundant Raw Materials, the Japanese are Very Satisfied. Promoting Military Industrialization Aims at Russia

Chengde Correspondence: Since the Japanese forcibly occupied Rehe, they have conducted detailed investigations into various agricultural and mining industries, and have actively developed them. Recently, they have conducted more detailed investigations into Rehe's industry. According to the Japanese announcement, although there are as many as 594 factories in Rehe Province, their total capital is only more than 692,000 yuan. The Japanese believe that this kind of small-capital industry needs to be controlled and improved, so that when conflicts occur with Outer Mongolia and the Soviet Union in the future, they can be manufactured nearby in the military industry for supply. This is the only purpose of the Japanese. The number of factories and workers in Rehe, as well as the amount of capital and output, are listed separately below:

Most of the above factories are in the scope of handicrafts. According to the Japanese, if Rehe's industry is developed and a special agency is formed for the puppet Xing'an Province, it will definitely be greatly developed. In addition, the position of the puppet Xing'an Province and Jinre can be determined. The Japanese also analyzed and statistically analyzed the industrial conditions of each county in Rehe Province as follows:

According to the above counties, the most developed industrial areas are Chifeng and Chengde. Chengde's leather industry is better than other places, so Chengde's leather industry has reached 26 factories. Leather is also one of the military industries, and the Japanese are very satisfied with it. Chifeng's industries, such as wool weaving, dyeing, pharmaceuticals, and winemaking, are developing as a whole. In the future, with the decision of the Japanese-planned Rehe economic policy, the prosperity of industry can be expected, as the Japanese boast. The development of Chifeng's gold refining plant is one example. In addition, the mining of natural soda, the production of saltpeter, and the basketry near the enclosure are all listed as special industries. Among them, many provide subsidies for the military industry. According to Japanese investigations, the main special industries in Rehe are as follows:

(1) Chengde's Nanmu industry: 3 factories, 15 workers, 140 yuan in capital, and 3,950 yuan in output.

(2) Lingyuan's gunpowder manufacturing: 2 factories, 15 workers, 400 yuan in capital, and 1,200 yuan in annual output.

(3) Chifeng's dyeing industry: 10 factories, 223 workers, 11.0 yuan in capital, and 76,150 yuan in output.

(4) Chifeng's pharmaceutical industry: 5 factories, 50 workers, 8.836 yuan in capital, and 41,000 yuan in annual output.

(5) Longhua's dyeing industry: 3 factories, 10 workers, 400 yuan in capital, and 2,850 yuan in annual output.

(6) Fengning's felt carpet industry: 3 factories, 10 workers, 1,190 yuan in capital, and 12,000 yuan in annual output.

(7) Luanping's pharmaceutical industry: 5 factories, 22 workers, 1.090 yuan in capital, and 600 yuan in annual output.

Songjiang: The Magistrate of Piyun Town is Found Not Guilty

Ding Shlong, the magistrate of Piyun Town in the First District, was ordered to handle the registration of opium addicts for self-reform, and he was quite conscientious. He was commended by the county government for his efforts. However, afterwards, Wang and Xu, claimed that their husbands had been detained for opium cases and that Magistrate Ding had been suspected of fraud. They filed a complaint with the provincial government, which ordered the county to investigate. The county government, on the grounds that the case involved fraud, sent it to the Songjiang District Court for investigation. The court found Magistrate Ding Shlong guilty and sentenced him to six months in prison. Afterwards, Magistrate Ding felt that he had made enemies with people for handling opium cases and that he had been framed. He was not satisfied with the verdict and hired lawyer Zhu Shaowen to appeal to the Suzhou High Court. After two hearings, he presented various counter-evidences. The debate ended on the 25th of last month. It has recently been learned from Suzhou that the High Court has overturned the original verdict against Ding Shlong.

Kunshan: Bandits Rob and Injure People in Nanwaitan

Zou Yuqing, the head of the first bao and ninth jia in Nanwaitan Village, Xinhui Township, District Eight of this county, is a farmer. Because his family is well-off, he was coveted by bandits. At about 11 p.m. on the 1st of this month, more than ten bandits suddenly came, broke into Zou's house with weapons, first tied up Yuqing and his sons and nephews, and then rummaged through the boxes and chests. They stole more than 200 yuan in cash and clothes and jewelry. However, the bandits were still not satisfied and forced them to say where the silver was hidden. They also struck Yuqing's chest with wooden objects, causing him serious injuries. The bandits then left. That night, the bandits went to the house of Rong Xiangsheng in the same village to rob property, but fortunately they did not injure anyone. After the bandits left, Yuqing was dying. He lingered until dawn on the 2nd and then died. After the county government was telegraphed for inspection, the body was coffined and buried.

Suzhou: Arresting the Principal Offender in the Murder Case

In the case of Ji Xia, the wife of Ji Zhongyuan of Lindun Road, being murdered by her lover, Yin Amao, near the Su-Kun Highway outside Qimen, Yin Amao fled without a trace. The police precinct arrested a suspect, Chen Gaisheng, in Wuxi and sent him to the district court for investigation. Because there was insufficient evidence of a crime, he was given a decision not to prosecute. According to a report from the family of the victim to the Public Security Bureau here, the real murderer, Yin Amao, has been arrested by the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau. They have requested that he be brought back. On the 4th, a document was prepared and personnel were dispatched to Shanghai to bring him back to be interrogated and dealt with.

Business Community Strictly Cracks Down on Smuggled Goods

The business and industry groups in Suzhou are sparing no effort in handling the prevention of smuggled goods. The County Chamber of Commerce, the General Labor Union, and the trade associations of Chinese and foreign cloth, silk weaving, and North-South goods have all organized anti-smuggling committees to strictly prevent smuggling. The County Chamber of Commerce believes that there are many difficulties in the actual procedures for implementing the "Measures for the Detailed Investigation and Clearance of Local Goods Made of Artificial Silk or Mixed with Artificial Silk" formulated by the Ministry of Finance. As it concerns anti-smuggling, representatives of the relevant industries and the Suzhou Customs Commissioner will be convened in the coming days to hold a meeting to discuss the matter. The anti-smuggling committee of the General Labor Union has assigned a large number of patrol officers to carry out inspections of smuggled goods, and on the 4th, it sent a letter to the Public Security Bureau, ordering all branches to assist the patrol officers in performing their duties in order to achieve results.

Water Police Arrests Two Notorious Bandits

Recently, robberies have been frequently reported in Su Township. It has been learned that the reconnaissance team of the Second Water Public Security District arrested three notorious bandits, including Liu Er from Jiangbei, on the morning of the 4th on the shore of Yangcheng Lake. They also seized a pistol and stolen goods. They were immediately escorted to the team headquarters for interrogation. After an interrogation, they confessed to having many accomplices. The team immediately dispatched personnel to arrest the remaining members of the gang. It is heard that the bandits are related to the robbery case in Weiting Township and are currently being interrogated.

Wuxi: Handling Household Registration Changes

Chen Yuchu, director of the Public Security Bureau of this county, recently stated that it is an essential factor in compiling baojia (neighborhood watch) that residents of each bao should issue a joint guarantee pledge, in accordance with the baojia laws and regulations. However, the investigation and reporting of household registration changes in the First District have been going on for several months, and there have been many changes in the residents' household registrations. The original joint guarantee pledge should be corrected as soon as possible to conform to the purpose of compiling and investigating baojia. However, the procedures for this matter are very cumbersome. It was submitted to the police affairs meeting for discussion and it was decided that each branch should conscientiously handle the matter in accordance with the joint guarantee pledge method. The joint guarantee pledge will be issued by the bureau.

Reorganization of the Land Tax Record Office

The County Government Land Tax Office previously had cases of stealing and colluding, involving many people, who were arrested separately, resulting in a major case. The county government is currently investigating, and the truth will soon come out. It is learned that Fang Guoding, the director of land tax, in view of the previous mistakes of laissez-faire and negligence, is trying to mend the fold. He has reorganized the collection office in a strict manner, merging the Yigui record room and the Yigui silver cabinet, and establishing three new shares: record checking, record management, and collection. Chen Bomiao was appointed as the head of the record checking share, Zhang Qiliang as the head of the record management share, and Zhu Songhuan as the head of the collection share. Deng Jiqian was transferred to the record checking share as a member, and Qian Bingqiu was transferred to the record management share as a member. Other staff members were slightly adjusted. For the sake of serious duties, each of the three heads was ordered to provide a written guarantee of 50,000 yuan, and each of the three members was ordered to provide a written guarantee of 5,000 yuan. The previous record checking room and silver grain cabinet were abolished.

Jiangyin: Summer Practices Autumn Orders Harming Cotton and Rice

Since the beginning of summer, it has been the Great Heat, and now it is the middle of the three hot periods. However, heavy rains have fallen from time to time, and the climate is as cool as autumn, resulting in poor development of morning crops, especially the cotton in the sandbar. It is most affected, because it is the time of flowering and fruiting. In addition, epidemics are prevalent, and people suffer from various diseases such as summer dampness and warm evil. If the sky does not clear up again, the autumn harvest will be inferior, and the farmers are worried.

Danyang: Chief of Education Bureau Gambles at Home

Yesterday afternoon, the Public Security Third Branch received reports from Xu Zhiben, Zhong Meiwu, and others that there was gambling and commission charging in Qin Manyuan's house in Wang Xiaozi Temple, No. 8, Jia 9, Bao 1, Siqian Town. Gamblers Qin Zhefu (i.e., Qin Manyuan, Director of the Education Bureau), Gao Lingxiao (i.e., Gao Duanyun, Principal of Quanzhou Primary School), Chen Zhaozhi (reportedly Chen Shizhang of the Education Committee), and Lu Zinan were arrested on the spot, along with gambling paraphernalia. Luhe: Brother Killing Case Has Been Verified

In Chliuliu Township in the Fourth District of this county, Chen Guochen, the fourth son of Chen Jichu, a local villager, had a long-standing feud with his third brother, Guofan. He took advantage of the opportunity to work in the wheat field a few days ago and killed Guofan with an axe, dividing the body into eight pieces and burying them. The wife of the deceased, Liu, heard the news and intended to go to the county to appeal, but was suppressed by her father-in-law, Chen Jichu, who sent people to monitor her, preventing her from taking action. Chen Mingluan, the head of the township, received a bribe of 50 yuan and did not come forward to report the matter, mutually concealing the crime. The county government learned of the matter through inquiries and immediately dispatched police to secretly summon the witnesses in this case for interrogation. The murderer, Chen Guochen, initially refused to admit it. However, as the interrogation continued into the night, Yang, the interrogator, ordered the electric lights to be completely turned off. At that time, the sky was dark and it seemed as if there were ghosts crying and gods wailing. The murderer was frightened and confused, and then frankly confessed. Liu, in order to seek justice for her husband, also confessed the true circumstances of the murderer's killing, and requested that he be punished according to the law. Chen Mingluan, the head of the township, for daring to take a bribe and conceal a major case of human life, should be severely punished. He has been temporarily handed over to the guarantee of three substantial shops, pending further summons for interrogation.

Nantong: Anti-Smuggling Operations by Land and Sea

The coastal and riverside areas of Nantong in Jiangbei have many remote, small ports where smuggling vessels frequently appear. They secretly transport goods inland for dumping. To protect the market, the various industry groups have formed an anti-smuggling committee. The Third District of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police has dispatched the "Jun He" and "Hai Ying" police vessels to patrol the rivers and sea to intercept smuggling ships. On land, the Public Security Bureau is conducting investigations.

Gaoyou: Canal Water Level Rising

Due to continuous rain in this county in recent weeks, the canal water level is rising daily as the Yi River flows into the canal. On the 2nd, the water level at the imperial pier was six feet eight inches (measured in construction feet). On the 3rd, it rose abruptly by one foot. According to the person in charge of the Jiangbao Section Office, although the water level is rising rapidly, there is no major concern at present. The county government has received an order from the provincial government to carry out flood prevention work and has formulated flood prevention measures for compliance.

Yangzhou: Continued Collapse of the Jiangxu Riverbank

Local figures in this county, such as Zhu Zhuxuan, concerned about the frequent collapses of the riverbank in the Jiangxu area, organized a committee to prepare for preventing further collapses. It is reported that the Jiangxu riverbank collapsed again yesterday, creating a dangerous situation. Upon hearing the news, the committee, represented by initiators Hu Xianbo, Dai Xingyi, Bao Xiangzhong, and Zhu Lizhun, crossed the river together on the 3rd to seek the agreement of gentry in Zhenjiang, such as Leng Yuqiu, Lu Xiaobo, and Yan Huiyu, so that Yangzhou and Zhenjiang can jointly appeal to the authorities to avoid further delays, which could pose a great danger to passengers traveling through Zhenjiang and Yangzhou. It is reported that the Yangzhou Progress Society also discussed this matter at length during a joint meeting of directors and supervisors yesterday and unanimously agreed to cooperate in addressing the issue.

Huaiyin: Public Security Bureau Arrests Opium Trafficker

The head of the Huaiyin Public Security Bureau, Lin Gubiao, ordered the arrest of opium trafficker Zhang Nianxin, but he had not been apprehended. Although there was a tip that Zhang Nianxin was hiding in Kongmiao Town in the first district, a police search found no trace. Now, this trafficker was selling opium outside the Wangying Beiwei gate in the third district on July 30th, with twelve taels and five mace of opium in his possession. The public security police discovered this and immediately rushed to arrest him at his address. Jiaxing: Several Days of Strong Winds and Rain

Jiaxing has experienced several days of strong winds and rain, causing many boats to capsize in the rivers. The river water has risen several feet. In the countryside, the mid-season rice is at the stage of heading, and the rain has caused significant damage. The late rice has not been greatly affected. The early rice that has already matured but not yet harvested has been damaged by the wind and rain, with the rice ears submerged in water, causing them to sprout. Low-lying fields have been flooded due to the rising water. Farmers are now draining the water to salvage what they can for the harvest. In addition, a considerable number of other crops have been damaged by the wind and rain.

Hangzhou: Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Plans to Build a Branch Line

The Ministry ordered the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway to construct a branch line from Zhangshu to Ganzhou. An engineering team led by engineer Wang Maoguan was dispatched to survey the route and has completed its work, returning to Hangzhou to report. It is understood that the line passes through the prosperous area of southern Jiangxi, from Zhangshu through Xingan, Xiajiang, Jian, Taihe, Wan'an, and reaching Gan County. The estimated length is over 310 kilometers, requiring an estimated construction cost of 21 million. The engineering work for this route is not particularly difficult. Funding is now being raised, and surveying is planned to begin soon. It is reported that Jian has a population of about 700,000 to 800,000, and Ganzhou has a population of 500,000, making the future business prospects promising.

Panic Due to Shortage of Autumn Silkworm Eggs

The Zhejiang Province had a bountiful spring silkworm harvest this year, and the price of silk was quite high, so farmers are very enthusiastic about raising silkworms. The total demand for autumn silkworm eggs ordered by various counties in the province is 90,000 sheets. The province can only supply 250,000 sheets, and about 600,000 sheets have been ordered from Jiangsu Province, leaving a shortage of more than 10,000 sheets. It is difficult to meet the demand, causing panic due to the shortage. The inspectors selected by the Silk Control Association have been dispatched to various counties to work. The distribution of silkworm eggs will begin after the 20th of this month.

Ningbo: Buddhist Association Plans to Build Barracks

The Yin County Buddhist Association, based on recent claims from major monasteries that their large temple buildings are often used for military deployment, while not hindering religious ceremonies, are actually inconvenient. The association, in view of this, purchased more than 20 acres of official wasteland on the Yinjiang Riverbank in the southern suburbs from the Sha Tian Management Office and plans to build 50 barracks specifically for military deployment in the future. They plan to submit a request to the county government for approval before proceeding.

Bandits Responsible for Multiple Kidnappings Executed

Xu Arong, Shan Yanling, Tang Jichang, and three other bandits, responsible for a series of kidnappings and killings within the Yin County over the past year, were captured by the Ningbo Public Security Bureau one after another and sent to the Yin District Security Command for trial. After confirming the facts through interrogation, they were submitted to higher authorities for approval. Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM, the three criminals were taken from the detention center, their identities confirmed, and under the supervision of Staff Officer Wang, they were escorted to the Caoma Road execution ground on the north bank of the river and executed by firing squad.

Dispute Over Unauthorized Dismissal of Township Head

Zou Keming, the head of the Zhouxing District in Yuyao, dismissed Shen Qinglin, the head of Zhonghe Township, without obtaining approval from the county government, which led to opposition from all the town heads and bao chiefs, who resigned en masse to the county government. Various merchants also jointly submitted requests for clarification. Local News

National Assembly Election Office Notice: Orders to Report Books and Records to Various Groups, Sends Personnel to Supervise and Assist

According to the National Society, the Shanghai Municipal National Assembly Representative Election Office is preparing for occupational elections. According to the law, each group must first prepare and submit its organizational charter and membership list to the election supervisor for review. Yesterday, it issued the second notice, with the attached forms, ordering compliance within ten days of receipt of the notice for submission and forwarding. The original notice and form filling instructions are recorded below:

Original Notice

"Shanghai Municipal National Assembly Representative Election Office Notice" (Second Notice) Regarding the notification matter, as stipulated in Article 20 of the Detailed Rules for the Implementation of the National Assembly Representative Election Law, "The election supervisor shall periodically notify each group within the original territory to prepare and submit the following types of books and records within the time limit and forward them to the competent election supervisor for review: (1) organizational charter, establishment procedures, and their history; (2) registration authority and registration date; (3) staff and their experience; (4) members' names, ages, addresses, native places, and the duration of their engagement in the occupation; (5) if a member is also a member of other groups, the name of the other group and the group selected in accordance with the provision of the "paragraph" at the end of Article 5 of the Election Law, in addition to distribution, a special notice is hereby issued to the association to prepare and submit all items of books and records in accordance with the above-mentioned regulations within ten days of receiving the notice for submission and forwarding. This matter concerns the electoral administration, and delay is not permitted. (Omitted below)

Instructions for Filling Out the Form

(1) For the "organizational charter" item, if the association has a printed charter, it is not necessary to copy it, just attach a copy. (2) For the "establishment procedures and their history" item, fill in the date of approval of the association, the preparation process, the date of establishment, the number of staff re-elections, and the current term. (3) For the "registration authority and registration date" item, just fill in the name of the registration authority and the date of registration. (4) For the "staff and experience" item, the names, experience, and positions of the association's staff must be filled in. (5) For the "duration of engagement in the occupation" item, if the duration of employment is interrupted, it can be calculated cumulatively. (6) In the membership list, the duration of engagement in the occupation should be filled in in the "remarks" column. (7) If a member is also a member of another group, the name of the other group and the name of the group participating in the election must be indicated.

Dispatching Personnel to Assist

The office believes that due to occupational elections, the number of agricultural and commercial groups in the city is very large, and the time is limited. Therefore, for the sake of speed, the office dispatched a large number of staff to various groups yesterday to supervise and assist in filling out the reports. The office has also begun the same notification for the election of free professional groups.

Consular Corps Still Insists on Revising the Labor Inspection Agreement; Regrets Obstructing Our Sovereignty; Municipal Government Submits a Request to the Central Government; Negotiations Temporarily Suspended

It was originally scheduled to be signed and implemented by both parties after agreement. Later, the consular corps of various countries suddenly expressed objections to the draft agreement and requested revisions, making it impossible to resolve the case for a while.
