Velvet Industry Anti-Smuggling Measures Approved by the Party Department; Contacting the Unified Tax Bureau Soon; Tax Certificate Issues Must Be Resolved First

The Shanghai Velvet Industry Association, in order to strictly enforce anti-smuggling, passed a resolution by the general meeting of manufacturers and members to organize an anti-smuggling committee, appointing Xue Yunsheng, Zhang Jinqing, Xu Jisheng, Xia Zirong, Wu Yunyou, Zheng Junzhan, and Hong Rouguan as the anti-smuggling committee members, responsible for carrying out anti-smuggling and combating smuggling. The anti-smuggling measures were decided to exchange fabric tax certificates for velvet tax certificates and to affix the seals of the weaving factory and velvet factory on the original tax certificates to prove their authenticity. After the anti-smuggling committee verified the authenticity, it affixed the association's seal and issued a transport order to be able to transport, as a fundamental way to prevent smuggling of fake and shoddy goods. Now, these anti-smuggling measures have been approved by the Party Department. The members of the association unanimously uphold impartial enforcement to benefit the national tax revenue and promote the sale of domestic goods. In order to actively prepare for the implementation of anti-smuggling, the exchange of tax certificates is the responsibility of the Unified Tax Bureau. It has been decided that the association will prepare an official letter and send representatives to contact the Unified Tax Bureau to exchange tax certificates. Once the tax certificate issue is resolved, the anti-smuggling work can be implemented.

State-Run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Reorganization Report

The state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company issued a report stating that since its reorganization, it has been making steady and tireless progress in reorganizing its business, equipping its ships, and rectifying its personnel. Its fundamental principle has been to maintain operations without neglect despite financial constraints. Although limited financial resources have prevented full-scale implementation over the past few months, gradual progress has been made and a preliminary foundation has been laid. Here is a report on the more important aspects and those that have already been implemented:

A. Business Reorganization

Reform of River Steamer System: Previously, all river steamers employed a comprador system with no restrictions on tickets, often exceeding cabin capacity by more than one or two times. Furthermore, vagrants and unruly soldiers mingled on board, smoking, gambling, and creating a chaotic scene. The ships lacked order, and hygiene was completely disregarded. Consequently, the treatment of steerage passengers on river steamers was almost inhumane. Each ship had usually one hundred and forty to fifty [tea] boys who were not paid wages. They relied entirely on privately selling bedding spaces and soliciting tips for drinks as compensation for their services. After purchasing tickets and boarding, steerage passengers had to buy bedding spaces from the tea boys to have a place to rest. Even the official cabins with fixed berths were often reserved in advance by those who extorted tips. The tip for drinks often amounted to more than thirty percent of the ticket price for long journeys and was even equal to the ticket price for short journeys, openly extorting money without any sense of shame. All of these shameful practices were unique to river steamers. Therefore, most travelers regarded river steamers as a long-distance [burden]. At the beginning of the reorganization, the company first implemented the elimination of these bad habits, uniformly replacing all ship compradors with business managers. Starting from April 1st, ticket offices were set up on the docks to sell tickets, and those without tickets were not allowed to board to prevent vagrants and unruly soldiers from mixing with the passengers. This also ensured that passengers arriving at the dock could purchase tickets without having to ask around. The number of tickets was limited to prevent overloading, ensuring that every ticket holder had a cabin space. Rules were established regarding the wages and drink tips of tea boys, prohibiting them from extorting fees from passengers. Furthermore, the New Life Movement Promotion Association dispatched members to reside on the ships and guide sanitation matters, which was widely praised as convenient. The company's passenger ticket revenue also significantly increased compared to before.

Abolition of Branch Offices: Due to financial difficulties, the company strived to conserve expenses. Branch offices or agencies in commercial ports where ships no longer sailed, such as the Chongqing Office and the Beihai Agency, have been abolished one after another. They will be restored in the future if ships sail to these ports again to avoid waste.

Suspension of the Inland River China Merchants Bureau: The Inland River China Merchants Bureau has consistently incurred losses over the years, and there have long been discussions about suspending its operations, but this had not been implemented. After the company's reorganization, permission was obtained to completely shut down, suspend navigation, and sell [assets]. The company is currently formulating detailed implementation measures in accordance with the Ministry's instructions.

Clearing Outstanding Debts for Passengers and Cargo: The company previously extended credit to various customers for cargo transport, sometimes exceeding the amount of the insurance policy, resulting in numerous store closures and significant losses. The recovery of debts was also difficult. After the company's reorganization, it formulated measures to restrict credit extensions while actively pursuing outstanding debts from various debtors or resorting to lawsuits in court to prevent excessive debt and facilitate clearing.

B. Ship Equipment

Installation of Radios and Amplifiers on All Ships: To ensure passenger safety, increase travel enjoyment, and facilitate the rapid transmission of navigation information, the company decided to install wireless radios and amplifiers on all river steamers to report the progress of the journey and broadcast music to entertain passengers at any time. The Xin Jiangtian and Jiang'an ships have already been properly equipped. The Jiangshun, Jianghua, and Haiyuan ships are currently being equipped. If the results are good, all ships will be equipped in succession in the future.

Installation of Ventilation Ducts on All Ships: To improve air circulation and sanitation in the third and fourth-class cabins, the company decided to install ventilation ducts on all ships, starting with a trial run on the Xin Jiangtian ship. The ventilation ducts on that ship have now been completed, and the Jianguo ship is also being equipped. It is planned to install them on the remaining ships in succession in the future. (To be continued)

German Leipzig Fair Welcomes China's Participation

Fixed Office Established in Hong Kong, Held Biannually in Spring and Autumn

The German Leipzig Fair is held biannually in spring and autumn. To welcome the participation of Chinese manufacturers, the fair has established a fixed office in Hong Kong with the address Leipzig Fair (Hong Kong office), Hong Kong. Chinese manufacturers who wish to participate in the exhibition can send a letter to that office for inquiries. The Leipzig Fair originated in the twelfth century. In 1197, Emperor Maximilian granted it a national protection certificate and government preferential rights. Subsequently, due to the passage of centuries, the Leipzig Fair acquired an international character and became the world's largest market for goods and machinery. Every year, over ten thousand manufacturers from around the world participate in the exhibition, and two to three hundred thousand merchants from various countries visit the fair for procurement. Therefore, the Leipzig Fair truly possesses great value.

Implementation Measures: The First Special District Citizens' United Association's Measures for Implementing Public Training:

1. These measures are formulated in accordance with the Shanghai Municipal Civic Training Implementation Measures and the Group Training Measures.

2. Committee members of the association and committee members of various district branches, or non-members, who are between the ages of eighteen and thirty-five, may register to join.

3. The training period is three months.

9. The registration and implementation dates and locations will be announced separately.

10. Matters not covered will be announced from time to time.

Grain Industry Requests Yard and Ministry to Salvage Wheat Outlets

Advocating a Way Out

The previous report stated that the mainland flour mills association requested a ban on wheat exports. A reporter from Da Gong She (L'Impartial) specifically went to the Shanghai Grain, Oil, and Cake Industry Trade Association to solicit their opinion. According to the person in charge of the association, the tariff policies of various countries are determined by the domestic supply and demand situation. For example, if the domestic production of a certain commodity is excessive, not only will export taxes be exempted, but the government will also provide special incentives for foreign trade to maximize exports. If our country sincerely wants to save agriculture, industry, and commerce, what other way is there than tariff policy? This year, the national wheat harvest is abundant, and production is extremely high. There are currently over 300,000 bags of wheat in Shanghai warehouses, and most of the wheat is still in the hands of farmers and is not easily sold. Domestic demand is limited. If a way out is not sought for such a huge surplus, there will inevitably be a risk of spoilage, which will harm the rural areas and violate economic principles. The association, seeing this, specifically submitted a report to the Executive Yuan's Ministry of Industry, requesting that measures be taken to salvage the situation. A copy of the submission is provided below: "Report on the fact that this year's wheat production exceeds demand, causing distress to both farmers and merchants, requesting that measures be taken to salvage the situation. The agricultural products of our country have always been dominated by rice and wheat. Since the imposition of import tariffs on foreign rice in 1933, the rural economy has gradually recovered. However, the rice harvest last autumn was abundant, and rice prices fell, which merchants already found painful, and farmers could not avoid being affected. This year's wheat harvest is abundant, the largest in recent years. Wheat production in various regions is extremely congested. Currently, Shanghai warehouses contain no less than 300,000 bags of wheat, and farmers who have not yet sold their wheat continue to ship it for export, seeking to sell it. The financial turnover is extremely hindered by such oversupply and huge surpluses. Merchants have to bear losses, and farmers cannot bear this either. The association believes that the price of domestic rice should be balanced as much as possible, and the outlet for wheat must be actively promoted. We hereby respectfully submit this report to the [Yuan] hoping that you will be mindful of the distress of farmers and merchants and quickly take measures to salvage the situation to avoid the risk of spoilage. We will be extremely grateful." Respectfully submitted to Chiang Kai-shek, President of the Executive Yuan, and Wu Dingchang, Minister of Industry, Shanghai Grain, Oil, and Cake Industry Trade Association, August 1, 1936.

National Products Promotion Association Requests the Purchase of National Products

If National Products Exist, Foreign Products Should Not Be Used and Reimbursed

The Shanghai National Products Promotion Association submitted a report to the Executive Yuan, stating, "Report requesting a reaffirmation of the government's previous order to purchase national products. If national products exist, foreign products should not be used and reimbursed." Ever since the opening of trade, the national industry of our nation, through the promotion and supervision of the government and the efforts of the people, has gradually taken shape after years of accumulation. However, the economic aggression of foreigners is all-encompassing. Initially, they competed with our young industry and commerce with their superior capital and exquisite goods across the sea. Later, when we raised tariffs and increased costs, they used unequal treaties as a shield, relying on their financial and intellectual resources to establish factories in the commercial ports of our country. Not only were they subject to the same taxes and levies as our national products, but they also relied on the special forces of the concessions to refuse to pay some or all of the taxes. With this superior position, their competition with our industry and commerce was invariably advantageous. This is the biggest reason why our industry and commerce have not made significant progress. Fortunately, in recent years, the government and the people have recognized that promoting national products is the only way to save the national economic crisis. The New Life Movement and the National Economic Construction Movement promoted by [Your] Excellency also listed the promotion of national products as one of their work guidelines. From then on, the government took the lead, and the people happily followed, and the future development of national products is limitless. The association is a joint organization of national product groups in Shanghai, and its establishment has been approved by the Ministry of Industry. Its internal work focuses on promoting and encouraging the use of national products. It is heard that the [Your] Yuan previously issued a notice to government agencies that they should give priority to purchasing national products for all needed items, which shows concern for the people's livelihood and is greatly admired. The association believes that this measure will promote the sales of national products and boost industrial development. However, the effectiveness of this order depends on the strictness of the supervision methods. After a collective discussion, it is proposed that the [Your] Yuan reaffirm the previous order for government agencies to purchase national products and strengthen supervision. In the future, if any agency purchases and uses foreign products instead of national product substitutes, the purchase should not be reimbursed, and the responsible personnel should be given appropriate punishment. This will allow national product manufacturers to develop slowly and steadily, and the entire national industry can be revitalized. [Your] Excellency has repeatedly shown approval for promoting national products. It is respectfully requested that you issue another clear order for its earnest implementation, which would be a great benefit." Respectfully submitted to the Executive Yuan of the National Government, Zhang Huikang, Hu Xiyuan, Lin Kanghou, Zhu Wenqi, and Wang Xingyao, Standing Committee Members of the Shanghai National Products Promotion Association.

No Need to Affix Stamps to Withdrawal Slips

Chamber of Commerce Responds to Leather Industry

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce yesterday replied to the Leather, Fur, Oil, and Bone Industry Trade Association, stating that there is no need to affix stamps to withdrawal slips used with passbooks. On the 3rd of this month, a letter was received asking whether stamps should be affixed to withdrawal slips used by bank depositors for transactions, even though they are using passbooks. Regarding this matter, the Ministry of Finance issued a directive on July 23 of last year, No. 6380, stating that the Shanghai Bankers Association has stated that a type of withdrawal slip used when withdrawing money from a passbook cannot be used to withdraw money solely based on the slip. It cannot be used externally and must still be used with the passbook to withdraw money from the original bank. Its nature is different from a check that can be used independently in the market. Since it cannot be used to withdraw money on its own, it does not fall within the scope of Article 16, Rate Table 4 of the new stamp tax and does not need to be stamped. The nature of the withdrawal slips used by banks with passbooks is no different from the withdrawal slips mentioned in the Ministry's directive. According to the aforementioned Ministry directive, there is no need to affix stamps. Moreover, the item of checks was also amended on February 10 of this year to be temporarily exempt from stamping. Therefore, the issues mentioned in the letter are no longer a problem according to the law.

Those who fail to report within the time limit will be regarded as electors of this association. This matter concerns the election and should not be delayed. Saving China's Silk Foreign Trade Requires the Transformation of New Style Silk Reeling Machines

The National Economic Council's Silk Improvement Association, the Silk Industry Department, and the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, in view of the huge volume of China's silk foreign trade, are taking measures to save China's silk exports. In addition to the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau's quality inspection of Zhumen bamboo silk exports starting from August 1, grading inspections of raw silk exports will be carried out again on February 1 of next year. It is also planned to improve the silk reeling machines in various silk mills to prevent China's foreign market trade from being taken over by foreign silk. It is found that 80% to 90% of the silk reeling machines in silk mills in Jiangsu and Zhejiang are Italian-style silk reeling machines, with some Japanese re-reeling silk machines. However, there are very few of the newest Japanese upright reeling machines. For example, in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, Shanghai Baotai and Yihe factories use Japanese re-reeling silk machines, and Wuxi Yongtai and Hangzhou silk factories use Japanese upright reeling silk machines. All the rest are old-style Italian machines. It has now been decided to find ways to transform the old-style silk reeling machines into upright reeling machines and to add new upright reeling silk machines.

Minsheng Company's Minben Ship Trial Run Yesterday

To be Handed Over to the Company for Acceptance at the End of the Month

The Minsheng Industrial Company, in order to develop Shanghai-Chongqing shipping, specially ordered two shallow-water river ships, named "Minyuan" and "Minben," from the Jiangnan Shipyard in Shanghai. They have now been completed one after another. The Minben ship held a trial run yesterday, with a speed of 13 nautical miles per hour. The Minyuan ship will also be tested within a few days. Both ships are scheduled to be handed over to the company for acceptance at the end of this month to operate between Shanghai and Chongqing.

Information from the Social Affairs Bureau States that Reports of Severe Illness are Inaccurate

Wu Xingya, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, took leave last month due to illness and went to Kuling for treatment. He is now gradually recovering. Impersonating Officials to Extort Money with Medicine: Hu Hengxiang Summoned Yesterday

Liu Wendao, our country's ambassador to Italy, whose Shanghai residence is located at No. 26, Lane 799, Haig Road in the French Concession, received a phone call at 4:00 PM on the 2nd of this month. The caller claimed to be sent by Wang Xiaolai, residing at No. 10, Huanlong Road, to deliver twenty bottles of refreshing medicine (痧藥水). After receiving the medicine, the caller requested a payment of twenty dollars to support charitable causes. Liu's family, noting that the master had no prior dealings with Wang, became suspicious upon receiving this unexpected call. They immediately contacted Wang's residence, where they were informed that Wang had no knowledge of this matter. It was then clear that the caller was an imposter attempting to defraud them. Shortly thereafter, a man arrived carrying twenty bottles of medicine and demanding twenty dollars. Liu's family detained the man and notified the Foch Police Station. Detectives arrived and took the medicine carrier and the medicine back to the station for interrogation. The man identified himself as Hu Hengxiang. He was detained pending further investigation. A brief account has already been published in this newspaper. Yesterday, the police transferred Hu to the Eighth Criminal Division of the Second Special District Court. Attorney Chen Ming of the Police Department presented the case, charging Hu with attempted fraud. A representative from Liu's residence appeared in court to testify about the defendant's fraudulent scheme. Shi Menglan also appeared on behalf of Wang Xiaolai, testifying that some time ago, someone delivered thirty bottles of medicine to No. 3, Henry Lane, Henry Road, impersonating Wang Xiaolai and defrauding him of thirty dollars. He also presented a letter from Jiang Jianbai, the third section chief of the Education Bureau, to Wang as evidence, requesting a severe punishment. The defendant Hu Hengxiang testified that he was forty-six years old and from Yuyao. He claimed that he was drinking tea at the First Spring Teahouse on Maidun Road that day when someone handed him twenty bottles of medicine and asked him to deliver them to Liu's residence, saying that he would be paid twenty dollars. He believed this to be true and went, not knowing he was being deceived and victimized. He did not know the person and did not know their address. Judge Qiu Huan-ying examined the testimony and ordered a postponement for further questioning in seven days. The defendant was returned to custody.

New Life Movement Promotion Association Inspects the "Three-ization" Life of Various Agencies

The Shanghai New Life Movement Promotion Association, in order to inspect the "three-ization" life (militarization, productionization, and artification) of various agencies, has specially prepared and issued performance report forms and is holding the third "three-ization" inspection. On the 3rd, a letter was sent to various agencies asking them to fill out the forms. Details are as follows:

Letter to Various Agencies

The association's circular to various agencies on the 3rd stated: "This association has been promoting the 'three-ization' life in various agencies for the fifth phase. In order to examine the current implementation, we have prepared a performance report form for Shanghai agencies implementing the 'three-ization' life. You are hereby requested to fill out the form within the deadline and submit it to this association to facilitate the New Life Movement."

Report Form Format

The report form is divided into: (A) General situation: 1. Does the head of the agency take responsibility for supervising and resolutely promoting the "three-ization" life among subordinates? 2. Is the overall attitude of staff towards the implementation of the "three-ization" life welcoming or indifferent? If they hold a negative attitude, what are the reasons? 3. Do staff members properly preserve and earnestly implement the key points issued by the association each phase? 4. When implementing the key points of the current phase, are the key points of the previous phase continued? 5. What kind of guidance and assessment methods does the head of the agency provide to subordinates regarding the implementation of the "three-ization" life on a regular basis? (B) Regarding militarization: punctuality, attire, office work, spirit, exercise, learning; (C) Regarding productionization: savings, allowances, income and expenditure, domestic goods, thrift, integrity; (D) Regarding artification: arrangement, attitude, speech, entertainment, conduct, mutual assistance.

Dispatch of Investigators

After the various agencies fill out and submit the forms within the deadline, the association will dispatch staff to conduct thorough investigations in various agencies to determine whether there are any false reports. After the investigations are completed, the reports will be submitted to the General Association. Therefore, this investigation is extremely thorough.

Reclaiming Lost Wealth: Chinese People Build Factories to Manufacture Automobiles Domestically; Main Factory Set Up in Zhuzhou, Hunan, Branch Factory Set Up in Shanghai; Within Two Years, One Hundred Vehicles Can Be Manufactured Each Month

According to the Central News Agency, thanks to the vigorous efforts in road construction in our country in recent years, land transportation has become frequent. However, the automobiles used are mostly imported from various countries, resulting in a huge loss of wealth each year. Recognizing this, domestic industrialists have initiated the establishment of a China Automobile Manufacturing Factory and have begun preparations, aiming to manufacture all components within five years and supply the people with affordable products. This is a newly emerging industry in our country and should be welcomed by the people. The reporter has learned the following details of the establishment plan:

The Amount of Wealth Lost Each Year Is Astonishing

Although automobiles have only been imported into China for three to four decades, the increase in recent years has been significant. In large cities such as Shanghai, Nanjing, and Guangzhou, the number of private automobiles has also increased year by year. Since the active construction of highways in various provinces, those open to traffic by the end of 1934 have reached more than 92,500 kilometers, and those in planning and construction have more than 68,000 kilometers. Due to the gradual development of highway transportation, the number of buses and transport vehicles running on highways has also increased rapidly. By the end of the same year, there were more than 50,000 automobiles in operation across the country, with Shanghai accounting for one-third of the total. Moreover, in recent years, the automobiles produced by various countries have been constantly updated, competing to be sold in our country, and the outflow of our money is alarming.

Factory Site Built; Completion This Year

Automobiles from various countries are powered by gasoline, and their prices are quite high. Ordinary passenger cars usually cost more than several thousand yuan, not to mention the daily consumption of gasoline. Because our country does not produce gasoline and must rely on imports from countries such as England, America, and Russia, domestic industrialists, recognizing this, initiated the establishment of the China Automobile Manufacturing Company, with capital set at six million yuan, which has already been fully subscribed. A preparatory office has been set up on Museum Road in Shanghai, and the main factory is set up in Zhuzhou, Hunan, with a branch factory in Shanghai. A factory site has been determined on Bansongyuan Road and construction is underway, which is expected to be completed this year. As for the components, they are ordered from Germany.

Complete Domestic Manufacturing After the Fifth Year

According to the person in charge of the company, the factory specializes in manufacturing buses and transport vehicles, using diesel or vegetable oil as power, the cost of which is only one-third of that of gasoline. In terms of manufacturing, because there is a lack of such engineers in China, an agreement has been reached with the German Benz automobile company to send several engineers to assist and guide. In the two years after the start of production, the engines and steel materials will be supplied by Germany, and by the fifth year, the engines and other components can be manufactured domestically. It is estimated that the selling price will be several times cheaper than imported products, and the production volume will be one hundred vehicles per month in the first two years. Afterwards, depending on the business situation, branch factories will be added elsewhere, and production will be increased.

Abductors Are Evil: After Two Girls Were Defiled, They Attempted to Sell Them to Dalian; The Two Girls, Seeing That the Situation Was Not Good, Cried Out Loud; The Police Detained Them and Transferred Them to the Court for Trial

The abductors Xu Weichang, 28 years old, from Yancheng; Qiu Lianfu, 35 years old, from Yancheng; Qiu's wife, Qiu Wangshi, 25 years old; the female abductor Li Wang Laoer, 43 years old, from Yangzhou; the Liang Lao Si couple and their 19-year-old son Liang Sugen; and a gang including Xu Xiaolong and Chen Hongchang, totaling many people, specialize in trafficking in human beings. They entice and defile women before selling them. Xi Kouhong, an 18-year-old woman from Yancheng, who lived on Zhongshan Road, Caojiadu, and Zhou Xiaomei, a 16-year-old woman from Yancheng, both worked at a medicine factory in Xiaoshadu. They met Qiu Wangshi and became acquainted. Qiu saw them as valuable commodities and became very friendly with them, eventually becoming close friends. On June 17 of this year, while working the night shift, they met Qiu, who, seeing an opportunity, hid the two girls' work account books under the pretext of looking at them. The two girls, trusting Qiu, said that their husbands had taken them. Qiu then said that their husbands were at their mothers' home in Jimo. The two girls, needing the account books for work, asked Qiu to go with them to retrieve them. They were lured to a room in the Zhongxing Hotel at the Grand Self-Ringing Clock on Laobshen Road, where Xu Xiaolong and Chen Hongchang defiled them. On the third day, Li Wang Laoer and Liang Sugen and others falsely told them they would be sent home. They drove to the Huangpu Wharf, intending to board a ship to Dalian to sell them. The girls, seeing that the situation was not good, cried out loudly and refused to board the ship. The police detained them and sent them to the police station, which then transferred them to the relevant police precinct. Unexpectedly, Xu Weichang, Qiu Lianfu, and Qiu Wangshi went to the two girls' homes, falsely claiming to have found them and extorting 5,000 yuan. They were then taken to the police station. The two parties met, and the truth of the case came to light. They were transferred to the District Court, where public charges were filed. Yesterday, Judge Zhang summoned them for questioning and ordered them to be returned to custody pending judgment.

Wu Rongsheng, a native of Yancheng residing at No. 150 Taoyuan Lane, Tiantong Road, was responsible for watching and protecting cargo being unloaded from large ships arriving in the Huangpu River and transported to the shore by barges. After Reorganization, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Has Made Great Progress in Its Business; There Is a Shortage of Ships on All Routes Due to a Surplus of Cargo; A Decision Has Been Made to Build New Ocean Liners

Since Zeng Guangqing took over as the director of the business department of the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, he has been planning to revive the business, advancing on the Yangtze River, South Seas and North Seas routes simultaneously. He has also added a Changsha route, reclaiming a large amount of transportation profits that had been flowing out. In March of this year, the company's Yangtze River shipping business declined for a time, but in the most recent two months, freight rates on the Yangtze River have been congested, and revenue has increased greatly. Among the six companies, it has jumped from sixth place to first place. As for the South China route, after the establishment in Guangdong, the exchange rate has stabilized, and customers have been rushing to stockpile goods. Cotton yarn, piece goods, and sundries are fully loaded on the Sihai and other ships each time they set sail, and customers still regret not being able to ship as much as they want. Director Zeng has decided to seize this opportunity to lease more ocean liners and assign them to the South China line to meet demand. At the same time, he is consulting with the shipbuilding department to quickly purchase new ships to strengthen coastal shipping. As for the North Seas route, which was hit by smuggling a few months ago, thanks to Director Zeng's efforts and personal involvement in cargo transportation, each time the Tianjin liner sets sail, it is fully loaded with grains and flour. In the past two months, the prosperous business of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company on the Yangtze River and the South Seas routes has broken all previous records, and there is a shortage of tonnage on all routes.

Two Ships Damaged Their Engines

Ningjing: The Ningjing ship of the Ningshao Company, which was sailing to Qingdao to transport coal to Shanghai, damaged its propeller while being towed to turn around and leave the dock when preparing to set sail from Qingdao on the 2nd. The tow rope got caught in the Ningjing's engine propeller, causing the propeller to jam. The Ningjing immediately stopped and dropped anchor. Divers were hired to enter the port, first remove the tow rope, and then find a way to sail. The damage to the propeller will be inspected and repaired after arriving in Shanghai.

Baofeng: The Baofeng ship of the Baofeng Company, which sails on the Chongsha route, was hit by a hurricane that swept through the port and stirred up large waves while approaching Chongming. Recent News on the Xu Wancheng Case: Appeal Filed Because Bail Was Denied; Jiangsu High Court Has Ruled to Reverse the Decision

Xu Wancheng, the owner of the Longwen Bookstore in Dama Gate, was sued for defamation and obstruction of official duties for publishing a special work journal that was deemed to have offended the Shanghai Local Court. He has been detained for two months. Cai Yuanpei, the president of the Academia Sinica, and others sent a letter requesting bail, but it was denied. Later, Xu's wife, Zhu Airu, appealed to the Jiangsu High Court. A few days ago, the High Court ruled that "The Shanghai Local Court's denial of bail in the Xu case is not fully in accordance with the provisions of Articles 117 and 114 of the Criminal Procedure Law, and it is a misunderstanding to use the danger of continued crime as a reason for not allowing bail and stopping detention, which is legally unfounded. The original ruling should be revoked and sent back to the original court for a new legal ruling." It is learned that after receiving this ruling from the Jiangsu High Court yesterday, Xu's wife has again requested the Shanghai Local Court to release her husband on bail.

Details were reported in yesterday's paper. According to a telegram from the captain of the Gongping steamer, which sailed to Guangdong in the same convoy, the Changde steamer sailed to the waters off Waitengshan (also known as Nanwudao) outside Shantou port. The Gongping steamer still saw the Changde steamer following behind. After that point, the Gongping and other steamers sailed to Guangzhou, and the Changde steamer disappeared without a trace. According to crew members of various sea-going vessels arriving in Shanghai from Guangdong yesterday, the ships had received telegrams requesting them to search and were actively searching the waters off Shantou and Fuzhou, but without any sign of the vessel. Even if it was sheltering from the wind, four days had passed by yesterday, and there should have been some news arriving in Shanghai. This reporter inquired with the company. As of 6:00 PM yesterday, there had been no telegram from the Changde steamer to Shanghai. Although the company is still constantly searching, the outcome is showing no possibility of a clue. The steamer's future is becoming increasingly concerning. If there is no news within the next day or two, it is feared that the situation is mostly inauspicious. In addition to the crew of over seventy sailors, there are also several hundred passengers on board, so all parties in Shanghai are taking this matter very seriously, constantly inquiring with the company about its whereabouts. It is heard that all crew members have a total of over 30,000 yuan in accident and life insurance.

A Thief Electrocuted to Death at Luen Cheong Weaving and Dyeing Factory, Discovered Due to a Power Outage, Body Was Charred Black, a Gruesome Sight

At 10:30 PM the day before yesterday, the lights in the Luen Cheong Weaving and Dyeing Factory in Lujiazui, Pudong, suddenly went out. The factory manager suspected that the main switch was damaged and urgently notified the Pudong Electricity Company to send a technician for repairs. When the technician arrived at the factory at 11:00 PM and was inspecting the problem, he suddenly found a black figure on top of the high wall by the river. He shined a flashlight on it and found a dead man clinging to the iron bar with both hands, his feet resting on the joint of a water pipe on the wall. His body was electrocuted by the main power line. The current was blocked, causing the outage. He immediately reported to the Pudong Branch Bureau, who summoned the local security chief, Lu Shunlong. Yesterday morning, he reported to the local court. At 2:00 PM, prosecutor Li Fen was assigned to cross the river to Pudong and ordered the body to be taken down. An examination of the body revealed a wound on the right back, about a foot long and seven inches wide, and eight inches deep. Another smaller wound on the right thigh, about a foot long and four inches wide, and two inches deep, was charred like charcoal. His whole body was black, and his lower body was completely shrunken. The skin was covered with small blisters. The death was extremely gruesome. No relatives were found to claim the body. He ordered the local security chief to prepare a coffin and bury it. As for who the deceased was, viewers speculated that he was a thief who had sneaked into the factory. Because it was late at night, he could not escape, so he climbed the water pipe to reach the top of the wall, intending to use the telegraph pole outside the wall to climb down. In a hurry, his back touched the power line, resulting in his death.

Central Bank Inspection Report

The 294th inspection report on the issuance reserve of Central Bank exchange notes states: "In accordance with Article 13 of the Central Bank Law, this committee is responsible for inspecting the amount of exchange notes issued by this bank and its reserve funds. We conducted the 294th inspection at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on August 1, 1936. The inspection results are reported as follows: (A) The total amount of exchange notes issued is 30,226,256 yuan in silver dollars, including 27,065,768 yuan in silver dollar notes and 3,160,052.88 yuan in subsidiary notes. The total amount of exchange note reserves is 30,226,256 yuan, including 20,233,7656 yuan in cash reserves in silver dollars. The cash reserve includes 10,676,033.79 yuan stored in the bank's issuing headquarters and branches, and 9,557,7322.21 yuan deposited with other banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 9,992,4700 yuan in silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold exchange notes issued is 400,963.07 yuan in customs gold. The total amount of customs gold exchange note reserves is 400,963.07 yuan in customs gold. This reserve includes 7,926.290 ounces of pure gold, priced at 51.68, equivalent to 400,963.07 yuan in customs gold. In accordance with Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve shall be at least 60%, and the remainder shall be the guarantee reserve in the form of legal guarantees. The results of this inspection show that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, and the guarantee reserve is within 40%, which complies with the regulations. This report is specially submitted. August 3, 1936, Li Fushun, Chairman of the Supervisory Board of the Central Bank, Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jilun."

Wu Lianzhou Discusses Damp-Heat Syndrome

Recently, there have been many cases of damp-heat syndrome, but few people understand its causes and symptoms. According to Wu Lianzhou, a national medicine doctor who provides voluntary service at this newspaper, the excessive rainfall during the moldy season increases the humidity in the air, and the hot summer raises the temperature. All indoor utensils, clothing, food, etc., have attached temperature and humidity. The warmth and moisture permeate the air, and we inevitably absorb it through our mouths and noses and then penetrate through our skin, causing the condition. In the initial stage of damp-heat syndrome, the body temperature reaches 103 or 104 degrees. Over five or six days, it becomes lighter in the morning and more severe in the evening. After more than two weeks, it gradually diminishes. After more than a month, the symptoms subside in the morning and return in the evening, and it takes more than a month to recover. The symptoms may include aversion to cold, headache, chest tightness, nausea, irritability, loose stools, dark urine, and the appearance of red rashes and white scales. In children, the onset is often accompanied by convulsions and coughing, and in adults, by throat swelling, coughing up blood, abdominal pain, vomiting, and diarrhea. These are signs of the onset of the disease and should be carefully examined and not misdiagnosed. Two colleagues at this newspaper, Wang Runfu and Ye Shaoqing, both suffered from damp-heat syndrome and were cured by Dr. Wu Lianzhou. Dr. Wu has extensive experience in treating damp-heat syndrome and his prescriptions are effective. His clinic is located next door to the west of this newspaper.

Datong Chemical Industry Factory Expands Operations

The Datong Chemical Industry Factory on Xie Xu Road in Nanshi, since its opening last winter, has produced various types of bakelite powder of excellent quality, which has been welcomed by manufacturers of bakelite products and eagerly adopted, recognized as equivalent to foreign goods. As a result, imports of foreign goods have been decreasing daily. The factory's current board of directors has also decided to increase the share capital by 30,000 yuan to expand the scope of operations. In addition to manufacturing various colors of bakelite powder, it will also add a section to manufacture raw materials such as galalith, in order to completely resist foreign goods. This is also good news for the future of domestic products.

New Business at Lu Tianbao Gold Shop - Serial Request -- Seeking Customers on Behalf of Customers

Lu Tianbao Gold Shop at Dapuqiao in the French Concession has established a serial request service, seeking customers on behalf of customers, to facilitate all sectors of society. The method of seeking is as follows: All ladies and gentlemen who wish to purchase high-quality, inexpensive ornaments, such as diamonds, jadeite, rubies, or sapphires, or customers who have the above ornaments and wish to sell them at a reasonable price, can write to the shop, but must clearly specify what ornaments they are and indicate the style and asking price. After receiving the letters, the shop owner will consider the situation of both parties and give priority to those who are closer. Then, a time will be arranged to introduce both parties for direct trading in the shop's reception room. Diamonds, jadeite, gemstones, and all gold ornaments will be appraised by experts. If a transaction is made, the shop will issue a guarantee of authenticity and value, charging only a 3% commission and no other fees. If the seller's ornaments are pawned, it can also be handled, but the amount of the pawn must be stated clearly.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 p.m. yesterday stated that the sky around Shandong was changing from overcast to showers, with strong northeast to northwest winds, due to a typhoon passing through the Yellow Sea and moving northeast by north. The sky over the upper reaches of the Yellow River was cloudy but still clear and calm with no wind. The lower reaches of the Yellow River and the upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River had slight showers with northeast winds. The sky over the lower reaches of the Yangtze River was cloudy with thunder. The wind direction was variable. The East China Sea had showers and strong southwest winds. The center of the typhoon moved to within 60 miles of 36 degrees north latitude and 124 degrees east longitude at 2 p.m., and the wind force has not subsided. Also, within the 24 hours before 3 p.m. yesterday, the temperature in this city reached a high of 87.8 and a low of 73.0. On the same day last year, the high was 91.4 and the low was 78.8.

Yarn and Cotton - New Cotton Dumped Cheaply - Forward Yarn and Cotton Heavily Sold Short

This is because the recent dumping of new cotton has been cheap, and some factories have purchased a lot of it. They have been heavily selling short in forward labeled yarn, and calculating the cost is profitable. As a result, the surface has loosened. As for the bulls, there have also been sell-offs, and the market price has become more and more unsustainable.

Seafood Sea Cucumber Faces Supply Discontinuity

Sea cucumber is imported from the East and West. According to industry sources, the total import volume at its peak reached forty to fifty thousand piculs, valued at five to six million yuan. Since the Customs began levying import duties, costs have increased, and foreign production has also significantly decreased compared to the past. A review of the total import volume for the past three years shows that it is less than half of what it used to be. However, prices for all types of goods have soared. New goods are currently being harvested in various regions, but the abundance of the harvest is still uncertain. The stock of old goods held by businesses in the city is dwindling, resulting in incomplete assortments of different grades. When customers need certain items, shortages are often experienced. During this period of supply discontinuity, the market situation for all goods is becoming increasingly tight.

The 11th Olympic Games, 1936: The Fourth Day of the World Games – Clear Weather, Owens Sets Two New Records, Stephen Wins Women's 100m in 10.15 Seconds, German Woman Creates 47.63m Discus Record

(Berlin) The enthusiasm of the audience on the third day of the World Games has not diminished, and the lively atmosphere in the stadium is quite amazing. Today the weather is clear, and the items attracting attention from spectators are the 200m, long jump, and women's discus preliminary rounds. (Another telegram) This afternoon, the program at the World Games stadium began with the 400m semi-finals. The venue was overcrowded, and German Chancellor Hitler also attended to watch.

(Berlin) The Olympic Games held the 200m preliminary round this morning. American black athlete Owens set a new Games record with a time of 21.1 seconds, but did not break the world record. (Note: The Games record is 21.2 seconds set by Tolan of the United States, and the world record is 20.6 seconds set by Metcalf of the United States.) This was one of the most exciting scenes this morning. The three Chinese athletes Liu Changchun, Cheng Jingguan, and Fu Jincheng did not place. Japanese athlete Taniguchi qualified with a time of 22.2 seconds. Then, the women's discus competition was held. Polish athlete Wega (name) Vanshana (surname) first broke the Games record with a throw of 44.69 meters. (Note: The Games record was 42.43 meters set by Vanshana.) But within minutes, German athlete More Mayu broke Vanshana's new record with a throw of 47.63 meters. (Havas, 4th)

(Berlin) Results of the middle hurdle finals: (1) Harding (USA), (2) Rawlins (Canada), (3) Hayward (Philippines), (4) Patterson (USA), (5) Padiha (Brazil), (6) Mantikas (Greece), time 52.4 seconds.

Women's 100-Meter Final: Ms. Stephens Wins Championship, Achieving a World Record of 11.5 Seconds, Preliminary Time Was Only 11.4 Seconds

(Berlin) Women's 100-meter final, American Ms. Stephens wins the championship, with a time of 11.5 seconds, a new world record. Second place goes to Poland’s Walasiewicz, third to Germany’s Krauss, fourth to Germany’s Dollinger, fifth to America's Rhodes, and sixth to Germany's Albus. (Central News Agency Special Correspondent Telegraph)

(Berlin) In the women's 100-meter final, American Helen Stephens won the championship with a time of 11.5 seconds. Polish veteran Walasiewicz came in second, and Germany's Krauss took third. (Reuters Dispatch on the 4th)

Berlin, 3rd (Reuters) - The only new world record discovered today was American Ms. Stephens' 11.4 seconds in the 100-meter preliminary round, the highest world record. The original record was 11.8 seconds set by Stanislawa Walasiewicz. China's Ms. Li Sen was in the same group as Poland's Walasiewicz. Ms. Li finished fourth, while Walasiewicz ranked first in this group with 12.5 seconds. Ms. Li was the smallest in stature and was in the lead at the start, but gradually fell behind.

These scores are calculated from the first to sixth place in each event's final, with the first place receiving six points and the sixth place receiving one point.

Owens Sets Another New Long Jump Record: Achieving 7.87 Meters, Our Country's Athletes Are All Eliminated

Berlin, August 4 (National United News Agency) - After breaking the 200-meter record today, American sprint star Owens also broke the long jump record. The new record is 7.87 meters.

Berlin, August 4 (Central News Agency Special Correspondent) - The Olympic long jump qualifying round was held at 10:30 this morning. Athletes were required to jump over 7.15 meters to qualify for the final. Our athletes, Wang Shilin, Zhang Jiakui, and Situ Guang, all failed to meet the standard and were eliminated.

Berlin, August 4 (Reuters) - In the long jump preliminary round, Chinese athletes Zhang Jiakui and Wang Shilin both failed to jump the qualifying distance of 23 feet and were eliminated.

Berlin, August 4 (National United News Agency) - The long jump qualifying round was completed this morning at the Olympic stadium. The standard distance was 7.15 meters. Those who qualified were Clark and Owens from the United States, Galardi and Muff from Italy, Beimer and Lischem from Germany, Tajima Naoto and Togami Kenji from Japan, Paul from France, Berg from Norway, Sosurka from Czechoslovakia, Ketke and Gester from Sweden, and Oliveira from Brazil.

200-Meter Preliminary Round: Owens Sets Olympic Record, Time is 21.1 Seconds, Our Country's Athletes Are All Eliminated

Berlin, August 4 (Reuters) - The Olympic record for the 200-meter was broken twice today during the preliminary rounds. America's Owens and Canada's Hembel each achieved a record of 21.1 seconds. The old record was 21.2 seconds, set by Tolan at the previous Olympic Games in 1932. Chinese athlete Cheng Jinguan was in the same group as Hembel, and Cheng completely failed, arriving last. Liu Changchun was in the same group as South Africa's Arni, with Liu finishing fifth and Arni winning with 21.7 seconds. In the fourth group, Switzerland's Heini was first with 21.9 seconds.

Berlin, August 4 (Haitong News Agency) - Today's most exciting competition was the 200-meter final. America's Owens broke the record with 21.1 seconds, Canada's Archibald came in second with 21.2 seconds, and Switzerland's Heini was third with 21.3 seconds.

Berlin, August 4 (Central News Agency Special Correspondent) - The Olympic Games held the 200-meter preliminary round at 10:30 on the morning of the 4th, divided into eight groups. Our country's athletes Liu Changchun, Cheng Jinguan, and Fu Jincheng all failed to qualify by about 10 meters.

Berlin, August 3 (Domei News Agency Special Correspondent) - The results of the first 200-meter preliminary round are as follows:

Women's Discus: Olympic Record Broken, Germany's Ms. Muiemeyer Throws 47.63 Meters

(Berlin, August 4, National United News Agency) - In the women's discus final, German athlete Muiemeyer broke the Olympic record with 47.63 meters. Poland's Wasuna won second place with 46.2 meters, and Mølenho third with 39.6 meters. Japan's Nakamura Niko came in fourth.

Hammer Throw Final Results: Top Three All Break Olympic Record

Berlin, 3rd (Domei News Agency) - The results of the hammer throw final are as follows:

1st Place: Hein (Finland) 56.49 meters (New)

2nd Place: Blask (Germany) 55.04 meters (New)

3rd Place: Hamberg (Sweden) 54.83 meters (New)

4th Place: Koering (Finland) 51.90 meters

5th Place: Wilhelm (USA) 51.66 meters

6th Place: Fibba (USA) 51.01 meters

The Olympic hammer throw record of 54.74 meters was set by American McGrath at the 5th Olympic Games in 1912. For over twenty years, no one had broken this record. Today, three athletes in the final simultaneously broke the record. Japanese athletes Abe and Matsuno participated in the preliminary round, with only Abe passing the preliminary round. However, in the final, his score was 49.09 meters, ranking 13th out of 17 athletes and failing to qualify.

Japan's Tetsuo Imai finished eighth in the second group. Hideo Tanaka did not qualify in the third group.

Weightlifting Final - Lightweight Division

Berlin, 3rd (Havas) - The Olympic Games' middleweight weightlifting competition was held this afternoon. The championship was won by French athlete Louis Hostin, whose total score for the snatch, clean and jerk, and press was 372.5 kilograms.

Berlin, 3rd (National United News Agency) - The lightweight weightlifting final was held tonight. The results are as follows:

Berlin, August 4 (National United News Agency) - The 400-meter middle hurdles semi-final was divided into two groups. The results are as follows:

800-Meter Semi-Final Results

Berlin, 3rd (Domei News Agency) - The results of the final 800-meter preliminary round are as follows:

100-Meter Final: Owens Ties World Record

(1) Owens (USA) ... 10.3 seconds

(2) Metcalfe (USA) ... 10.4 seconds

(3) Osendarp (Netherlands) ... 10.5 seconds

Berlin, 3rd (Reuters) - Today, in front of tens of thousands of spectators and Hitler, American black athlete Owens won the 100-meter final with a time of 10.3 seconds, tying the world record. Second place went to Metcalfe, also an American black athlete, and third to the Netherlands' Osendarp. America's Wykoff came in fourth, Germany's Borchmeyer fifth, and Sweden's Stenlund sixth. All six got off to a fast start, with Owens and Osendarp taking the lead early on. In the final 40 meters, Owens flew ahead. Metcalfe, relying on a final surge, finished second by only a shoulder's length. Metcalfe's time was 10.4 seconds, and Osendarp's was 10.5 seconds. The competition was held in a brisk wind, and it was nearly dark. Owens ran in the first lane.

Berlin, August 3 (National United News Agency) - In the men's 100-meter final, American athlete Owens won first place with 10.3 seconds. The audience numbered over 100,000 people, and Chancellor Hitler was also present. Second place went to America's Metcalfe with a time of 10.4 seconds, and Dutch star Osendarp was third with 10.5 seconds. America's Wykoff was fourth, Germany's Borchmeyer fifth, and Sweden's Stenlund sixth.

The starting positions, from inside to outside, were as follows: Owens, Stenlund, Borchmeyer, Osendarp, Wykoff, Metcalfe. Owens and Osendarp had the fastest starts. After 60 meters, Owens began to take the lead, and Metcalfe also worked hard to move forward, so he was ultimately able to surpass Osendarp. The 100-meter final was the most exciting event of the second day. The champion's time tied the world and Olympic record.

The International Sports Association has now decided not to recognize the 10.2-second record set by Owens in the preliminary round on Sunday, because "he was aided by the wind."

Fencing Semi-Final

Berlin, August 4 (National United News Agency) - The men's fencing semi-final was held this morning. The results are as follows:

Germany defeated Belgium 10-2, with 60 touches against 64 touches. France defeated Argentina 12-4, with 45 touches against 71 touches. France is currently in the lead in the second group with two wins. Germany and Belgium each have one win and one loss. Argentina has two losses. The German team still needs to compete against Argentina, while France will compete against Belgium.

Italy is in the lead in the first group, defeating the American team 13-3. Italy defeated the American team with 52 touches against 74 touches. Hungary and Austria each scored 8 points, but Hungary had 53 touches, while Austria had 63 touches. Therefore, Italy has two wins and no losses, while Hungary and Austria each have one win and one loss. America has two losses. The matches between Italy and Austria, and Hungary and America, are yet to be held.

Olympic Contributor: Count Coubertin Sends Congratulatory Telegram to Hitler

Berlin, August 3 (National United News Agency) - Honorary President of the Olympic Games, Count Coubertin, sent the following congratulatory telegram to German Chancellor Hitler at the opening of the Games: "As the Olympic torch shines in the Berlin stadium and Your Excellency announces the opening of the 11th Olympic Games, I am deeply impressed by the greatness of this preparation. In my later years, I deeply feel that Germany's support for my work has been increasing with time, which makes me extremely gratified and moved." The German Chancellor replied in a telegram saying, "Thank you very much for your congratulatory telegram. The entire German people believe that being able to promote Your Excellency's immortal work and the Olympic spirit at the 1936 Olympic Games is an unparalleled honor."

Preliminary Soccer Matches: Italy Wins 1-0 Against the USA, Norway Wins 4-0 Against Turkey

Berlin, 3rd (Havas) - Preliminary soccer matches were held this afternoon, totaling two games. Italy defeated the United States 1-0, and Norway defeated Turkey 4-0.

Grand Opening of Sailing Competition: British Cruiser Participates in Ceremony

Kiel, Germany, August 4 (Havas) - The Olympic Games sailing competition is scheduled to be held here today. The authorities specially held an opening ceremony last night. The port was brightly lit, dazzlingly. The Olympic torch was relayed from the capital to this location and raised to the mast of an old-fashioned seagoing vessel docked in the harbor. At the same time, the warships "Emden" and "Niobe" in the harbor flew the Olympic Games flag. In addition to the participating athletes from 26 countries, Admiral Albrecht, commander of the German Baltic Fleet, Admiral Forst, naval commander, and many naval attachés from various countries also attended. The United Kingdom specially dispatched the cruiser "Neptune" to arrive in this port, and presented a clock from the German armored warship "Hindenburg" (which sank itself in the Scapa Flow after the end of the European War) to the German Navy. In addition, Italy will also send a cruiser to this port to participate in the grand ceremony.

Sailing Postponed Due to Wind

Kiel, August 4 (National United News Agency) - The Olympic yacht race in Kiel was originally scheduled to start at 10:30 this morning. However, due to a storm and dangerous waves on the sea, it has been postponed to 12:30. Although the weather is not ideal, the yachtsmen in the harbor are applying oil to their bodies, preparing to resist the raging storm.

Educational News

When Revising Elementary School Regulations, Special Attention Should Be Paid to the Following Points: Ministry of Education Issues Order to Education Departments and Bureaus of Provinces and Cities

The Ministry of Education issued an order on the 3rd to the education departments and bureaus of provinces and cities, stating, "Since the implementation of the Elementary School Regulations, there are practical aspects that must be revised. The Ministry has made appropriate revisions, which have been announced under Order No. 10680. The points that should be noted are listed below: (1) Elementary schools and affiliated elementary schools of provincial and national universities and colleges should, in accordance with Articles 12 and 13, report the student roster to the local county and city education administrative organs and submit the experimental plans and results to the Ministry annually for verification. (2) The number of students in elementary schools should comply with the provisions of Article 20, ensuring that it is sufficient. If necessary, the principle of exceeding the regulations may be applied. (3) Elementary schools should uniformly comply with the provisions of Chapter 5, merging subjects, reducing time, and researching and improving teaching materials and methods. However, after the reduction of teaching time, the original number of teachers need not be reduced, so that their teaching burden is lighter, and they can share school affairs and moral education matters, and engage in research and further study to improve themselves. (4) The methods for calculating the academic performance of elementary school children, the methods for evaluating physical education, and the methods for promoting or retaining children should be formulated and reported as soon as possible in accordance with the provisions of Article 47, if they have not yet been formulated and reported, and submitted to the Ministry for record. (5) Elementary school graduation examinations should no longer be held in the future. (6) Elementary schools should, in accordance with the provisions of Chapter 10, set up free school places. Without prior approval, no tuition fees or any other fees may be charged. (7) The appointment, treatment, and protection of elementary school teachers should be handled in accordance with the provisions of Chapter 11. The request for registration of qualified teachers shall not be rejected, and advancements and retirements shall not be subject to changes due to changes in principals or responsible educational administrative personnel. (8) Elementary school principals should be carefully selected in accordance with the provisions of Article 64. Only in places where it is impossible to appoint qualified personnel may the provisions of Article 66 be followed to make flexible arrangements. (9) Provinces, cities, and counties that have not yet organized elementary school education research associations should organize them as soon as possible in accordance with the provisions of Chapter 12 and conduct research. In addition to separate orders, a full copy of the revised Elementary School Regulations is attached, and it is ordered that it be strictly followed, and that all subordinate elementary schools be ordered to follow suit. This order is hereby issued."

Shanghai City's One-Year Report on Implementing Free Education (II): Last Year's Free Education Expenditure Totals 150,000 Yuan; This Year, the Central Government Approves an Allocation of 120,000 Yuan

(G) Awards and Penalties: In the first semester of the 24th year, the following five schools were commended for their diligent work: Shihua, Haishan, Wanzhu, Feihong Elementary Schools, and Xinlu Normal School. The following ten schools were warned for their poor performance: Qingwei, Zhangmen, Ditang, and Caocun Four Short-Term Elementary Schools, Caonan, Yongxing, Yinxi, Longhua, Wusong, and Tangpan Six Elementary Schools. Zhangzhai Elementary School's attached class, which was the least diligent and had no results, was ordered to be closed. In the second semester, the following four schools were commended for their diligent work: Shihua, Wanzhu, He'an, and Yude Elementary Schools. The following five Short-Term Elementary Schools were warned for their poor performance: Kangqu, Yangzhai, Jiangzhai, Ditang, and Caizhai. The following thirteen schools were warned for their poor performance: Dexin, Zhongshan, Yinhang, Shagang, Juequn, Renji, Yongning, Neidao, Aizhen, Xincun, Honglu, Caonan, and Yinxi. Aidong Elementary School's attached class, which was the least diligent and had no results, was ordered to be closed.

(2) Promoting Elementary Schools: In the first semester of the 24th year, a total of three elementary schools were added. One is Xincun Elementary School, one is Zhangzhai Elementary School, and one is Meiyuan Elementary School. There are a total of five regular grades, three short-term elementary school classes, and one two-part system grade. Excluding the number of students in the short-term elementary school classes, it can accommodate 350 children.

(3) Expanding Existing Grades: In the first semester of the 24th year, a total of 27 grades were added, and in the second semester, a total of 16 grades were added, for a total of 43 grades, which can accommodate 2,150 children.

(4) Vigorously Implementing the Two-Part System: In the first semester of the 24th year, a total of 27 grades were added with the two-part system, and one grade was added in the second semester, for a total of 28 grades, which can accommodate 2,800 children.

(5) Improving Private Schools: This bureau has made every effort to reorganize private schools. In the first semester of the 24th year, the registration of private schools began. A total of 295 schools were registered, and personnel were immediately dispatched to investigate in preparation for improvement. (1) The shortcomings of private schools found in the investigation are mostly: (1) The school buildings are not hygienic; (2) The facilities are too simple; (3) The teachers' knowledge is too low; (4) The teaching materials are inappropriate. Due to the above situation, this bureau decided to reorganize and immediately opened a training class for private school teachers to provide training. A total of 237 private school teachers participated in the training. The training lasted for three months, and 210 people passed the exam, and 27 people failed. The qualified personnel have been issued certificates by this bureau. Wu Xiang and 69 others were rated as Grade A. Wang Zhongqi and 58 others who were absent without reason have been ordered to suspend operations. Qiu Jianzhang and 12 others whose grades were too poor have been ordered to suspend operations. Fang Yonghong and 26 others who were absent from class too much were considered to have failed. This bureau has separately awarded and punished them and severely cracked down on bad private schools.

(5) Trial Implementation of Mobile Education: This city is trying to implement mobile education vehicles to go deep into rural areas to work. Three mobile education vehicles have been set up, each vehicle with a standard of 50 students. The structure and equipment of the vehicles are under the responsible guidance and design of Committee Member Tai Shuangqiu of this association. It is now planned to add electric lights or gas lamps to the vehicles and hang them in the middle of the top of the vehicles for teaching at night. However, the equipment is not yet ready, and nighttime work has not yet started. Starting from the 25th year, it is planned to increase the number of vehicles and further promote this method. A total of 150 children have benefited from the mobile education vehicles. (7) Trial Implementation of Extracurricular Free Education: This bureau has formulated various regulations for extracurricular free education and is preparing to implement them. The current methods have been filed with the Ministry of Education and the Municipal Government. Starting from the 25th year, Gaoqiao District will be designated to start the trial implementation.

General Review of the Past Year

Since the implementation of free education in this city, there have been many difficulties and obstacles in promoting free education. We have used administrative power to minimize some of them, but we have not been able to do it smoothly. Let's calculate the total:

(1) Number of Children: Short-term elementary schools and short-term elementary school classes account for 7,166 people, the promotion of elementary schools accounts for 350 people, the expansion of existing grades accounts for 2,150 people, the vigorous implementation of the two-part system accounts for 2,800 people, and mobile education vehicles account for 150 people. Adding the number of children in expanded existing grades, the total is more than 14,000 people, which is in line with the original plan. (2) Stepping up supervision of schools: The bureau assigned two staff members to specifically oversee, guide, promote and improve free education. Ordinarily, each school must report the grades of students on a score-by-score basis once, and each school conducts home visits. The schools generally are able to make progress step by step.

(2) Solving the difficulties that can be solved: Compulsory education in this city has begun to be implemented for almost a year. The bureau provides immediate guidance and solutions to the practical difficulties encountered by each school. For larger issues, they are submitted to the Free Education Association for discussion. For example, children are often absent, so it is stipulated that students be retained. Children's progress is uneven, so multiple teaching methods should be used. Homework is delayed, so spring break and various holidays are not allowed, and intensive tutoring is given to achieve the planned goals.

(4) Paying attention to rewards and punishments: The personnel engaged in free education work have half the obligation and are more hardworking than ordinary education workers because the children they come into contact with mostly come from poor families. Therefore, for these children with poor family education, the measures taken for management, teaching, and hygiene are more laborious and may not necessarily achieve equally good results. At the same time, because it is a new matter, the facilities and treatment are not the same as ordinary elementary schools, so it is very difficult to achieve good results. This bureau will, of course, provide teachers with as much convenience as possible in all aspects for general children, but teachers must also do their best to serve the society. To encourage them, this bureau has established a system of rewards and punishments to supervise them at any time. In short, the above is a general report on the implementation of compulsory education in this city in the 24th year. For a detailed report, this bureau has printed a "General Report on the Implementation of Compulsory Education in Shanghai," which is currently being typeset. We hope that educators across the country will provide guidance on any inaccuracies. (End)
