Spring and Autumn

Snippets

— (Zhang Feng)

Those who have a home are tired of it, while those who don't long for one, just like those who have relatives are tired of them, while those who don't long for them, sharing the same psychology.

Many who have a home think of it as a burden—a heavy load that's not easy to carry, enough to ruin the future of those with ambition, and entrap the integrity of the honest!

Those who don't have a home mostly admire it as a blessed place—a soft and comfortable setting, enough to comfort you with contentment, and encourage you to move forward with excitement!

Those who have a home but cannot return to it recall the happiness of family life in the past, and dream of it constantly. Those who are away from home as guests are envious of the harmonious family situations of others, especially during festivals. Those in difficult circumstances hold negative views, thinking that things would be better if they left home. In short, things are done by people, and feelings change with circumstances. In fact, a home can be neither loved nor hated.

People endure hardship and toil to make a home, like silkworms spinning silk to make cocoons, settling themselves in a small world organized by themselves!

On the Pillow

— Sleeping Buddha

When we put our heads on the pillow, it should be entering the most peaceful and restful state; however, the opposite is often true. When you are busy with work, you feel muddled, neither happy nor sad. But as soon as your head hits the pillow, thoughts, memories, regrets, plans, joys, sorrows, fears... all rush in like a tide. It makes one suspect that this brain, the seat of thought, is not in our head but on the pillow; otherwise, why would it exert its authority and function so greatly as soon as it touches the pillow?

Even if our brain is not on the pillow, I think the pillow should at least be the key to our brain. When this key opens the door of thought, no matter what you hide in the deepest layer, the old and long-lasting shadows and feelings will be brought out without omission. At the same time, if you want to conceive or plan something on the pillow, you will have good success. The ancients had already discovered this. The ancients said that poetry is composed in three "shangs," one of which is "on the pillow." Other examples include improvisations on the pillow and idle chants by the pillow, which often produce better poems. When I was studying at home, I had such a habit: whenever the old teacher gave me a composition topic, I would first spread out the paper and dip the brush as usual, but in the end, I would often scratch my head and not write a single word. So I would run to the bed and lie down, raising the pillow higher. After thinking for twenty or thirty minutes in this way, the complete draft would be ready in my mind, and then I would write it out and submit it, and it would often win praise. Later, composing on the pillow became my "pillow secret" for writing compositions.

In middle age, although I still make a living by writing, the happiness of composing on the pillow has long disappeared. Now, the thoughts stirred up on the pillow are dissatisfied memories and fears of the future. However, I always feel that I have failed the pillow.

Therefore, I think the best use of the pillow is for planning. Isn't everything in front of us in need of planning? So I hope everyone will "raise their pillows higher" and generate some plans on the pillow.

Toilet

— Mani

Because what a person excretes has a special smell, it must be placed in a container. This container for storing feces is called a toilet bowl, and the place dedicated to human excretion is the toilet.

In Shanghai, not to mention that earning money is not easy, even excretion is troublesome because you can't excrete on the spot, you have to go to the toilet. And toilets in Shanghai are really hard to find. If you come to Shanghai for the first time, it is difficult to solve the problem of excretion. Even if you find a toilet, you have to buy a ticket (toilet paper) to enter. After all, Shanghai is a civilized place.

Excreting in the toilet, squatting down and putting on a stinky face, seems uncomfortable. Excreting in the toilet bowl at home is always uncomfortable with the smell. Because of this, there are people who have studied the toilet bowl and tried their best to invent a flush toilet, which has no odor, is very comfortable, and is extremely clean. Only a toilet expert can think of a flush toilet.

Shanggang, thirty miles northwest of Yancheng, Subei, still uses the old method because science is not well-developed. The toilets have separate rooms and seats, which are very comfortable and very clean. At each toilet door, there is a plaque with the names Osmanthus Hall, Osmanthus Pavilion, and Yibu Building. Although Shanghai has flush toilets, they are only for the enjoyment of noble people. Toilets like those in Shanggang are suitable for both refined and popular tastes.

Female Salesperson

— Zhu Ying

The fragrance of wine, the aroma of meat, the sound of dice throwing, and the laughter filled the East Flower Hall of a certain restaurant when suddenly, a girl carrying a large rattan basket in her hand, dignified and lively, came in from the windows and doors, stood still, put the rattan basket on an empty table, opened the basket lid, and took out some things from inside and placed them on the table.

This girl looked to be only eighteen or nineteen years old, her face was neither long nor short, perfectly fitting the standard of an oval face. Her skin was quite fair and delicate. She had a little lipstick on her lips. Her hair was loosely permed and tied with a red ribbon. Her figure was so slender. So as soon as she entered the door, she silenced the shouts of more than thirty gentlemen-style guests in the whole room, who rushed to the empty table, surrounding the girl with concern. Old Grandpa Li, who was over sixty years old, Old Xu, who was limping, Dr. Yang, who often cursed women, and Director Wu, who claimed to have never been interested in women in fifty years, all squeezed into the crowd, craning their necks and staring desperately.

"What's going on? What is she doing here?" Little Yu, who was particularly short and had thick glasses on his nose, squeezed behind the people, desperately trying to push forward, asking this question.

"A salesperson from ××× Pharmacy, selling ×× pills," the person standing in front told him. Then, the female salesperson also opened her mouth, using a rhythmic tone, skillfully and pleasingly describing the effectiveness of the medicine and the low price. Finally, she looked around with a pair of black eyes hiding under her slender eyebrows, and raised several packages of medicine, waiting to be purchased. But none of the thirty or so gentlemen made a move, except to look at each other.

"Hehehe, Miss, if you can drink a glass of wine for me, I promise to buy three packs from you?" Little Yu squinted his eyes behind the thick glass lenses and said, breaking the surrounding silence and causing everyone to laugh. Everyone laughed heartily, preparing to see the female salesperson's embarrassment. But unexpectedly, she not only did not show any embarrassment but even stretched out her hand to ask for wine. She not only drank the glass given to her by Little Yu but also drank six or seven glasses in succession. Later, she simply picked up the wine pot, poured herself a glass, and led everyone in the room to toast her. Laughter rang out again in this East Flower Hall, mixed with the female salesperson's loudest laughter.

Finally, she placed three large packages of the medicine she was selling in front of everyone. Everyone had to obediently take out one yuan of legal currency. Before long, she sold more than thirty yuan, thanked everyone happily, and went to sell elsewhere with her rattan basket. After she left, Little Yu suddenly clapped his hands on his legs and exclaimed in surprise, "Oh, I forgot to ask her what her name is and where she lives!" His face, full of wine, showed a look of frustration, followed by another burst of hearty laughter from everyone.

Goldfish Musings

— Wu Jiren

Grafting goldfish, as I mentioned briefly in my previous article, I have tried it this spring. At this time, the young fish are beginning to show their characteristics. There are several types, including "bubble-eye evert", "five-flower piled jade", "blue piled jade", "western egg bubble", and "western egg skygazer". After repeated selection, only a few are neat and beautiful. I am still glad that I have not given up hope.

"Five-color small goldfish" are a mixture of blue, purple, five-flower, western dragon, and western egg varieties. Because the blue and purple varieties are naturally colored when they hatch, they are particularly beautiful. As for the five-flower, western dragon, and western egg varieties, they are also colored from a young age, unlike other varieties that do not change to red until three to five months later. Mr. Xian Guansheng, feeling that "five-color small goldfish" can be used to decorate elegant rooms, specially ordered thousands of high-footed glass cups to hold the colorful fish, which are displayed in the six stores of each branch, and the price is very low, to attract customers to use them as a refreshing pastime in the summer.

Mr. Zhou Jianyun, manager of the Star Film Company, returned from Europe and the West with Hu Die, loyal to the silver kingdom, and improved the Star. He worked hard for a year and finally succeeded. This time, he recruited talents extensively and expanded greatly, especially credited with labor. Furthermore, he does everything personally and has no spare time. Recently, he has eliminated unnecessary social interactions and spends his free time cultivating fish and birds for regulation. Those who enter his room see brocade scales splashing and good birds chirping, and can imagine his elegance. Mr. Zhou once visited western aquariums, saying that the fish tanks there are built into the walls, with whole pieces of glass on the left and right, with water stored inside, and decorated with electric candles, so that the special swimming fish are all visible. The bottom of the water is covered with colored stones and planted with algae, as if one is in the seabed. The water is constantly flowing, so the fish are safe, and planting algae is also for ventilation. Now, his residence has two glass tanks, one for European tropical fish, with various colors and more varieties than our Chinese goldfish, and one for Chinese five-color goldfish, with no less than ten varieties. Because the equipment is beautiful and the water is clean, it is pleasing to look at.

Mr. Zhu Wanming, a magnate in the dyeing industry in Shanghai, is deeply interested in raising fish in his spare time. He values the quality of fish over the quantity. He once told me that if you want the fish to be fat, you can buy rice wine, remove the coarse particles, and then steam it in a rice pot. Give it a little every day, which is better than giving it water maggots every day. Don't change the water too often, but add clear water every few days. The results have been very good for the past two years. The fish from last year have now grown to five inches. It is not easy for a private fish to grow so large.

The book "Goldfish Raising Method" is more practical and has become very popular. Now, the third edition is published. Now that the mildew season has just passed and it is easy to raise goldfish, all my friends in Hao Liang should have a copy in hand. Those who send ten cents of legal currency to Yanling Jilu, No. 269 Dajie, Caohejing Town, will immediately receive a copy.

A Phoenix Replaces the Nest

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter 4: Sight and Sound are Fleeting Doubts Recur; Life and Death Can be Entrusted, Generously Sending Dirges

When I returned home in the evening, I met Miss Li on the road. I greeted her respectfully, and she seemed very sincere. Seeing the joy on her face, it was even more evident that she had no malicious intent when she questioned me about the paintings. Actually, I was dizzy as if I were drunk, and then I fell into deep thought again. When the evening lights came on, my thoughts became obsessive, and I didn't know what I was trying to do, so I circled around your neighborhood three times. In the dark alley, two people bought lamps to go to the market, and they whispered that Miss Li's pain came from living in a small building, opening the window to admire the moon all night. I thought to myself, who else but you could have such different views. Outside your house wall, there is a small garden with two tall willow trees. I stood under the willows and looked around, and I could see a corner of the small building, with the lights dimly lit. I knew it was meaningless, but I didn't understand why I was doing it. It's just that you can know that what I seek is comfort for my soul, not to be a frivolous and unrestrained person. This matter is not worth telling you, because telling you might only increase your avoidance of me. However, from now on, I will never do it again. Since you don't allow me to write letters, I shouldn't write this letter, but I am sending this letter to show the readers that I am not discouraged by your rejection of me. After you receive this letter, it's okay if you don't see me, and it's okay if you greet me with anger, but I know that you like to read the novels I write, so I will try harder to create more refined works to meet your expectations. Although there have been these two letters back and forth, I worry that you may no longer like to read my articles because of this. However, this is not something I can worry about. I think that if this can slightly comfort my soul, I will do it, otherwise, I will be unable to arrange myself. I don't know if the sick Miss Li I heard about is you. If it is you, then I dare to say that you should strive to be strong, eliminate your hidden pain, and fight for freedom. If you need anything, I will go through fire and water without hesitation. I have written thousands of words, but I still haven't expressed my full meaning, so I will write a short poem to make up for it.

I wish to be a green-feathered bird, nesting in the willow outside your building, without fearing the peach and plum trees, watching the door all day long.

I wish to be a purple bronze mirror, placed on your dressing table, serving your appearance all year round, not allowing any dust to fall on it.

I wish to be a blue frost sword, accompanying you on a long journey in the sea of people, flashing a three-foot light, cutting down injustice for you.

I wish to be the moon in the sky, reuniting every year, forever illuminating the pearl curtains, not allowing you to be unhappy.

I wish to be a monthly rose, blooming every morning in the old garden, meeting you every day, always making you happy.

I wish to be the wind and clouds, making your steps quick, not worrying about the bumps in the road, stepping onto the path of freedom.

I couldn't sleep all night, and my sorrowful thoughts surged. I still want to say more, but I fear my words will be messy. However, with just these few poems, I see that life and death can be entrusted. Knowing me or blaming me, I will prove it in the future. Respectfully presented to Miss Li, Jian, Litian bows a hundred times (57)

Special Writing

The Life After Joining the Farmers' Ranks

— Song Tingdong

One of the hottest mornings, school started its summer vacation. Many students packed their luggage, busy going home. Only a few of us intern students, carrying extremely simple luggage, took rickshaws and set off towards the remote countryside.

Among these students, some wore worried expressions, knowing there would be more hardship than joy in this trip; others were very happy, because they had already made up their minds, preparing to bury themselves in hard work. As the vehicles passed through the city and arrived in the vast countryside, some students even fell asleep in the rickshaws. The remaining few talked and laughed, encouraging each other not to become rural locusts on this trip.

Upon arriving at the experimental district, the director-general assigned each person a place for their internship. After eating lunch in the district, we immediately parted ways. In that moment of separation, we were truly saddened, unable to express the feelings in our hearts.

I was assigned to the Dangli Dang Fourth People's School. As soon as I entered, I was shocked. Inside were broken tiles and dilapidated walls, truly resembling the mountain villa for coffins at the foot of Mount Hui. The bedroom could only accommodate a bed, and the damp, musty air constantly surged into my nostrils, making it hard to breathe. Recalling the time when I lived in the school dormitory, complaining about the bad screens and mosquito bites, complaining about the simple facilities and lack of hygiene, compared to this, there was truly a world of difference.

It has been two weeks under these living conditions, and I already feel very comfortable. I have gotten to know many old farmers, and several village children have become very close to me. They all said in unison, "This teacher is not bad at all."

The life in the countryside is originally very interesting. When your spirit is comforted, coming to this countryside and being with the old farmers, not admiring vanity, not loving prosperity, the natural beauty of the clear morning and moonlit night is truly endless to appreciate. In the city, there is truly a sense of sitting in a well and looking at the sky. In the countryside, looking far and wide, there is no end in sight. White clouds rise, changing in a myriad of ways, unfathomable; the setting sun is about to fall, the sky is full of red neon, breathtakingly beautiful. Cicadas on the trees and frogs in the fields sing to each other, calling for prices to be heard, truly making you feel that the music in the movie theater is unbearably vulgar. By the clear stream, you can practice swimming; on White Dan Mountain, you can train for a healthy run. When tired, you can take a nap in the forest; when in high spirits, you can help the farmers plant rice in the paddy fields. In the bamboo forest, under the roots of old trees, sipping fragrant tea and reading newspapers, isn't this a wonderful realm? The joys and sorrows of life originally have no standard. At the same time, because each person's concept of enjoyment is different, the sufferer thinks it is joy, and the joyful thinks it is suffering. Who is right and who is wrong? This can only be understood and appreciated by each person themselves.

There are many problems with farmers in the countryside. As long as you are willing to study them, problems are everywhere waiting for you to solve. There are many social evils in the countryside. If you are willing to work hard, there are careers everywhere waiting for you to strive for. One afternoon, I participated in the founding meeting of a cooperative. Their spirit was very good, and the discussion items were quite organized. In my heart, I thought, who says the Chinese people are hopeless? It's a pity that these useful people have never been noticed! They asked me to give a speech. Although I was not prepared, I was very willing to tell these pure and lovely people: first, the organization must be strict; second, things must have a beginning and an end; third, they must be able to sacrifice private interests for the public good. They were very happy. Finally, the discussion of cooperative farming methods and the method of purchasing bean cakes in batches were quite appropriate. As long as the people who lead the Chinese people are willing to sacrifice everything to be their mentors and put their energy as much as possible into them, after a year, the power of the Chinese people will be cultivated. Who would dare to covet us? I don't believe that China will always be the oldest, useless, invaded, and trampled on. As long as we have knowledgeable mentors, make up our minds, and work hard to awaken the people, sacrifice our energy, and train a large number of promising people, the revival of the Chinese nation is bound to be hopeful! Friends! I hope you can all make up your minds and strive towards this path. Empty talk is not enough to save the country. Only burying yourself in hard work is a down-to-earth method! Friends! I represent the farmers in welcoming your arrival!

Page 18

How to Save the Misfortune of National Products

— Yimin

In the last ten days of last month, representatives from chambers of commerce in various provinces and cities held a joint meeting in Shanghai. In addition to passing important resolutions such as organizing the Committee for the Inspection of Smuggling in Various Regions of the Republic of China and petitioning the Ministry of Finance to temporarily postpone the levy of income tax, there was also an extremely important resolution, which was to request the government to issue an order to protect the transportation and sale of legitimate goods.

The so-called legitimate goods undoubtedly naturally refer to national products. In recent years, the matter of promoting national products has changed from the cry of a few people into a widespread movement, from the promotion in cities to affecting towns, almost everyone knows it. However, up to today, why has the national product industry not progressed and even deteriorated? Some say that because national products are poorly manufactured and expensive, the blame lies with the industrial and commercial sectors. Others say that most Chinese people lack a national concept, only seeking cheapness. They think that all foreign goods are good, and they don’t care about the impact of using foreign goods on the country. Therefore, the nationals who purchase foreign goods should bear the blame for the declining national product industry. Both of these statements can be said to be reasonable, but they are not the most fundamental reason. The fundamental reason is that the government has not been able to provide sufficient convenience and maintenance for national products everywhere!

First, let's talk about factories. We know that anyone who runs a factory, unless they are mentally ill, who wouldn’t want their products to be better than other people's? But in fact, some national products are indeed of poor quality. What is the reason for this? To answer this question, we can explore the reasons why foreign goods are excellent. It is said that the government spares no effort in maintaining the manufacture of foreign industrial products. If there is a shortage of capital, you can ask the government for help. If there are foreign goods coming to compete, the government will find ways to resist them for you. If there is any new invention, the government will give you a bonus. If you want to promote sales abroad, the government will help you in front. They have all kinds of conveniences, so naturally they can not worry about everything and wholeheartedly study the manufacturing of products. And what about our Chinese factories? On the one hand, they have to plan the turnover of finance, and on the other hand, they are worried about the market being taken away by others. They have no surplus funds to equip new machinery and recruit specialized talents, and they have to reverse the cost and cannot use good raw materials. As a result, naturally, they can only act hastily. To say that factories have no responsibility at all is certainly not possible; but to say that factories deliberately produce shoddy goods is not reasonable.

Secondly, let's talk about commercial firms. To be honest, the purpose of merchants selling goods is to seek profit. As long as that kind of goods is cheap to buy and easy to sell, they will import that kind of goods. This is naturally very reasonable. Because national products have heavy taxes and high manufacturing costs, merchants abandon them and choose foreign goods that are easy to sell. Are they unpatriotic? I dare not say that there are no people who are willing to be traitors; but I believe that most commercial firms are reluctantly abandoning national products. Finally, it is time to talk about users. Among users, except for a part of quasi-traitors who are superstitious about foreign goods and put the country and nation behind their minds, 99% of them have no choice but to purchase foreign goods. Because foreign goods use unequal treaties as a talisman, the taxes on their sales in our country are lighter than those on our own goods. In addition, their governments reward them with refunds of raw material taxes, so their prices are cheaper than ours, and the quality is excellent. In this way, Chinese people will naturally adopt them. If we say that patriotic compatriots should endure the pain and pay a high price to purchase national products, this cannot be done, and even if it can be done, it cannot be maintained permanently. Because it is human nature to be greedy for cheapness, and the quality is good; you tell him to abandon cheap and good foreign goods and not buy them. It is said that it is still ineffective in advanced countries where the level of people's knowledge is higher than ours. To tell greedy and foolish Chinese people to pay a high price to buy inferior goods is simply an idiot's dream!

Therefore, don't talk about promoting national products, otherwise, we must first ask the government to maintain them. In recent years, although the government has been much more concerned about the national product industry than before, the obvious ones, such as the number of highways established in various provinces, the abolition of likin, the reform of the currency system, and the holding of industrial mortgage loans, have all been implemented one after another; however, this is not enough. What the industrial and commercial sectors urgently hope for at present is to refund raw material taxes, cut and eliminate transit taxes, thoroughly eliminate the exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous taxes of disguised likin in various provinces, reduce national land and water transportation costs, increase import taxes on foreign goods, and eliminate tax evasion and smuggled goods. Only in this way can the misfortune of national products be saved, and only in this way can there be a glimmer of hope for national vitality!

The time has come to the final life-and-death juncture. With the greatest enthusiasm, we hope that the wise government authorities will adopt and implement the requests of this joint meeting of the chamber of commerce.

Industries That Can Be Done What Others Have Not Done

— Yang'an

—Olympics and Mr. Wu Yun Chu—

Our national products participated in the International Labor Olympic Games last year. Among the first-class awards won, the award recipient was designated as Mr. Wu Yun Chu, manager of Shanghai Tianchu MSG Factory. This award was sent by the chairman of the conference to our embassy in Belgium and then transferred to our Ministry of Foreign Affairs, which then sent it to the Ministry of Industry for distribution. On the sixth of last month, the Ministry of Industry held a special award ceremony. This glorious event is not only the honor of Mr. Wu alone, but also the glory of all of China and the entire nation.

I once said that Chinese people like to speculate, imitate, enjoy the existing situation, and do things that everyone does. Therefore, in any industry, there are fewer inventors and more copycats, fewer successful people and more failures. Especially in today's national product industry, whenever a new industry emerges, countless people envy its huge profits, and then follow suit, resulting in supply exceeding demand, and the result is that everyone perishes together, or gives foreign goods an opportunity to take advantage of. The lack of protection for inventors and the difficulty in creating new businesses are extremely heartbreaking to say. If this kind of bad mentality is not eliminated one day, it will not be easy to develop the Chinese national product industry one day.

Mr. Wu Yun Chu has been engaged in the chemical industry for more than 20 years. He has a great interest in chemistry and has made many contributions. In total, the businesses he has initiated, such as Tianchu MSG, Tianyuan Hydrochloric Acid, Bleaching Powder, Caustic Soda, Chichang Colloid, and the recently opened Tianli Nitrogen, are all industries that others have not done, industries that are not easy for others to do. He does not imitate or speculate. He has gone through countless difficulties and used countless spiritual strengths to manage diligently and achieve success. Moreover, these several industries are all basic industries of the country, industries that are extremely related to national defense, and have made great contributions to society, the country, and the nation. This is truly worthy of admiration and worship. The Olympic award is just the beginning. I deeply hope that Mr. Wu will continue to build on his interest in the chemical industry. In the future, the society's reward and commemoration of Mr. Wu, as well as the country's and the world's rewards and encouragement to Mr. Wu, will be limited? Or even more, "Shun is also a man, and I am also a man. If he can do it, I can also do it." I hope that domestic chemists, as well as all industrialists, will make good use of their brains and spirits, think about creating, think about inventing, and follow in the footsteps of Mr. Wu, and also have all kinds of construction, and be able to do industries that others have not done, to repay society, the country, and the world, and to wash away the shame of Chinese people who only know how to enjoy the existing and do not know how to create. Then the brilliance of China's new industry will be even more brilliant. In the history of inventions all over the world, we Chinese will occupy a huge page. What kind of glory is that? Encourage Mr. Wu, encourage the country's chemists and industrialists, they also hear the wind and rise up, and continue to make progress?

The Mat Industry in Taizhou

— Sun Linchang

Taizhou is located in the territory of Lin'an County, Zhejiang Province. Its terrain is backed by mountains and faces water. It has always been known for producing mats. Therefore, among all grass mats, there is the name Taizhou Mat. However, mats sold at sea are proclaimed as Taiwan mats. However, they do not know that Taiwan has no mat grass and no one weaves mats. Therefore, the word "Taiwan" is actually a mistake for "Taizhou." This may be because the original perpetrators showed an exaggerated tone because Taiwan was farther away, so they used it as a slogan. Later generations have accumulated habits and followed suit. The word "Taiwan" has almost become a fixed term for grass mats, while the real Taizhou mats are buried and not known. Therefore, I especially correct them here.

Taizhou mats have fine, long, and soft mat grass, so the products are smooth and durable. The diameter of the coarse side of the mat is woven from Longxucao grass. This grass is produced from local mountain valleys, shaped like cattails but fine. Taizhou mats have these two characteristics, so they are not as good as other mats.

The raw materials for Taizhou mats are planted by local farmers. Each household has several mu or dozens of mu. Sowing in early spring and harvesting in autumn. After drying, they can be applied. The weaving machine is made of wood, with a simple structure, shaped like the character "井". There is a wooden shuttle and a bamboo Tongcao knife. When weaving, one person holds the shuttle and one person passes the Tongcao. The days are long in summer and autumn. Each machine can weave four mats per day. The days are short in spring and winter. Also, because the weather is cold and frozen, the mat grass must be soaked in water before it can be applied. Therefore, each machine can only weave three mats per day. On average, each machine can produce more than 1,280 mats per year. According to the calculation of more than 1,530 machines in the whole county, 1,960 bundles of mats should be produced each year. (100 mats per bundle) In addition to selling this item to neighboring counties, local people mostly hoard them at home, waiting for mat vendors to buy them and transport them to Shanghai and Hangzhou for resale to various ports.

Promoting National Products is Not About Just Talking

— Master of Yiyiguan

"Promoting national products is not about just talking." In other words, "promoting national products" requires practical work. It is not just empty words that can achieve results.

Originally, we Chinese people only have one mouth, which is the most brilliant. No matter what, not only is it this matter of "promoting national products," they only know how to talk about it, but do not know how to do it in practice. Therefore, for decades, everyone still cannot help but shout the slogan of "promoting national products" to persuade people to promote "national products." And there are still "foreign goods" for sale on the market, and there are still people who want to buy "foreign goods!" Thinking about it carefully, this cannot be blamed on everyone only knowing how to talk about it, but not knowing how to do it in practice.

I remember someone once said this: "The British only do and don't talk, the Germans do and then talk, the Japanese talk and then do, and the Chinese only talk and don't do." These few words really hit the nail on the head! Looking at it this way, what else is there to blame for the fact that others are getting richer and stronger every day, while we are getting poorer and weaker every day?

Alas! Now let's stop talking nonsense. In short, even if we cannot "only do and don't talk," even if we cannot "do and then talk," well, at the very least, we should "talk and then do," and don't always be like this "only talk and don't do."

You must know that if you "only talk and don't do" in everything, you will "achieve nothing in your life." Especially "promoting national products" is not just about relying on one mouth!

Shen Bao This City Supplement

Talks

Talking About the Inheritance Tax Issue

— I

Yesterday, I wrote an article about Chen Jitang crying, which led to the recent government's plan to actively plan to collect the inheritance tax. Mr. Chen is a good example of a deeply poisonous inheritance. Inheriting property is an unearned right, but in modern social and economic theory, it should be taxed. Therefore, advanced countries not only attach importance to inheritance tax, but also regard inheritance tax as one of the country's important tax sources. According to economists, inheritance tax has the function of controlling capital, developing social production, and eliminating national dependence and promoting self-reliance. This is the result of economists' theoretical research, and their statement is naturally correct.

But I think this is not a fundamental solution. The fundamental solution is to simply abolish the inheritance system. Therefore, collecting inheritance tax not only has various troubles, but also has many drawbacks. There is no accurate investigation of national property in our country, and there is no regulation for registering inherited property with the government. Moreover, inheriting property is an old system inherited from thousands of years ago in our country. Once inheritance tax is collected, the national economy will inevitably store more money in foreign banks to avoid national collection, or use the names of other people's property to circumvent it. Secondly, inheritance tax only collects a part of it, and there is still a large part of it as inheritance, so descendants can still enjoy wealth and honor, and live a luxurious life. The grandfather should accumulate more wealth. The more wealth accumulated, the more the tax collection can make descendants enjoy endlessly.

I don't understand economics, and I don't understand the principles of economic operation. However, according to the current economic situation in our country, saying that collecting inheritance tax has the function of controlling capital and developing social production, I dare not say, and saying that it can eliminate national dependence and promote self-reliance is even more difficult to say. Therefore, I say that collecting inheritance tax can increase the country's economic income by a large part, but saying that it can control capital and develop production is just a tax term. Because the capital of our country, according to the current situation, should be increased as soon as possible, let alone control it, and the development of production should also depend on the method and purpose of production.

Therefore, my proposition is not to oppose the collection of inheritance tax, but to go further and simply abolish the inheritance system. Human beings are originally selfish animals. Seeing Chen Jitang's recent affairs and the situation of society, most of them are the result of the inheritance system. It is really necessary to abolish the inheritance system. The so-called inheritance is to leave it to the children and grandchildren, and to the great-grandchildren and great-great-grandchildren, and to the infinite grandchildren. Therefore, the more wealth accumulated, the wider and farther the inheritance left. Therefore, unscrupulous exploitation and demand, and harsh collection, the more harmful and the more numerous. If the inheritance system is abolished, then we will know the uselessness of accumulating capital and the uselessness of collecting money, which is enough to reduce the greedy desires for taking and demanding. Not only will the economic concept be slightly less valued, but also the idea of harming others and benefiting oneself can not arise, that is, public undertakings and social production can also be developed because of this. If the country's income is more and more, and there are fewer and fewer social wealthy slaves, isn't this a win-win situation?

Breaking Ground

— Zhifu

I

At dawn, the people at the foot of Eagle Claw Mountain woke up, like wild birds, crawling out of the low thatched huts one by one.

They were always paying attention to the road construction project. Recently, the Liu supervisor had come to the foot of the mountain and said to the people:

"... We braved the hot weather to measure the wasteland, lay a monument, delineate the boundaries, and mark the lines... Now the work can be considered complete. On the half of June, we will start breaking ground. The procedures for assigning labor and compiling schedules can be announced immediately! This section of Eagle Claw Mountain is assigned to the two supervisors, Lao Liu and Guo Ma's Face..."

His words were exciting. The people at the foot of the entire mountain stared at each other, waiting for - the half of June - the auspicious day for breaking ground.

On the eve of this near date, they sharpened those iron shovels, hoes, and digging tools to a shine. The entire valley was filled with the clanging sound of metal.

Everyone's desire grew stronger -

"When the work is completed, we will enjoy ourselves! We will communicate with the outside world, we will be... we..."

"But, when can it be completed? Dad..."

"Soon!..."

The resident living in the hillside slope, the old farmer Weng Ahu, who was born like a yellow wolf with a head full of white hair, felt a more joyful thirst than others. His son, Xiao Atu, smiled with a thin black face, playing with the iron digging and questioning him.

Although they could not understand everything clearly, a kind of strange expectation filled the minds of the father and son...

A very comfortable early wind blew, and the bright red small flag inserted on the top of the mountain fluttered, almost shaking people's eyes in a chaotic manner.

Paying attention to the vicinity of the red flag, you can also find the white, sheep intestine-like powder road. Guo Ma's Face and others had been doing these jobs on the mountain a few days earlier.

People will use these lines to flatten it with hoes and sweaty blood...

II

An unprecedentedly excited commotion of the people of Eagle Claw Mountain unfolded at noon that day.

Supervisor Liu, Lao Guo Ma's Face, and a group of about ten people, wearing straw hats, arrived at the foot of the mountain when the sun climbed over the roof ridge.

Wearing two iron carts of tools, full of bamboo baskets, mud baskets, carrying poles, bronze stoves...

"Folks! Breaking ground today..."

"We gather at the mining area at the foot of the West Mountain... Brothers!"

Sharp voices shouted at the same time:

"Supervisor Liu! Which section are we assigned to work?"

"Wu Li Gang..."

"Start cultivating the land!"

"Breaking ground... first chop down trees..."

"Oh!..."

So, people returned to the doors of the thatched huts, carrying hoes on their shoulders, and walked excitedly towards the foot of the mountain...

In the vast open space, people gathered one after another, like ants. The air became tense! The widespread human voice spread from the noisy foot of the mountain.

Everyone in the village was so crazy that they almost danced with joy.

The surroundings became quiet as if they had been acupuncture, and even the towering Eagle Claw Mountain was as quiet as a kind old man, piously praying for their expectations!

One Foundation Hard After measuring and delineating the boundaries, a stone tablet with gold characters is erected. This procedure is commonly called - laying a foundation.

Two Color Line Use lime to wipe a white boundary line on the boundary line of the road construction.

Three Breaking Ground This is a common custom. Before starting work, a "breaking ground" practice must be performed, similar to the current popular - ribbon-cutting ceremony, unveiling ceremony... similar customs.

If the Young Masters Return to the Countryside

— Hong

Our Country's Beekeeping and Rabbit Raising Industry (Part 1)

— Fei

(Special Report from This Newspaper) Our country is very suitable for beekeeping, both in terms of geography and climate; and beekeeping is not only easy to manage, but also does not require a lot of capital. As long as the area is rich in nectar sources, with a few hundred dollars of capital and five acres of land, a beekeeping field can be opened.

Beekeeping is a good rural sideline, its profitability is excellent, and it is also very helpful for flowers and fruits; European and American countries not only vigorously promote beekeeping, but also equip bee colonies near every orchard to increase fruit production. However, the general farmers in our country lack common sense and think that bees are harmful to fruit trees; although some people raise one or two colonies of bees, they only keep them for fun and do not know how to manage them. As a result, they all escape and die.

The first person in our country to advocate improved beekeeping was Mr. Hua Yizhi. In the first year of the Republic of China, he raised Italian bees in Xinzhi Dangkou Town using new methods. Up to now, the number of bee breeds promoted in the Yangtze River and South China areas is no less than 30,000 to 40,000 boxes, and the establishment of beekeeping fields in various places is almost like bamboo shoots after a rain. Those who have achieved results include Lida, Qingchun, Dazhong, Hua Yizhi, Xiaonong, Gan Yongmao, and other beekeeping fields, namely the Zhonghua Bee Breed Improvement Field. They all have a relatively long history in the beekeeping industry.

Among the bee breeds, the Italian bee is the best. There are currently about 4 million boxes of this bee colony raised in the United States; our country has a vast territory, abundant flowers and plants, and if we can promote breeding, it is not difficult to exceed this number.

The average annual honey production per box is about 50 catties, and the average value of every 100 catties is about 20 to 30 yuan.

Honey has a wide range of functions. In addition to being used in Chinese and Western medicines, cosmetics, candies, tea cakes, and cakes, it can also replace sugar, and can be used to make honey wine - Mr. Jiang Hongze of Lida School sells real honey wine, which is made using his own invented "honey wine making method" (now available for sale at Lida Farm). It can be used to make honey tea. In German villages, honey tea is served to guests. - It can be used to make tonics, and it is better to mix it with milk to feed children. Honey is a semi-digested product, so it will not cause diabetes, and it will absorb moisture and has the effect of relieving cough.

Second-grade honey is also good for making machine oil, which will not solidify in cold weather. It can also be used to make shoe polish. Loquat, lychee, longan, and orange honey have a very clear, fragrant, and sweet taste, and can be made into honey tea to replace coffee and tea.

In addition to the many functions of honey, beeswax also has many uses. For example, chemicals and medicines also need beeswax. It is also said that the value of pure beeswax is also very expensive.

The distribution of honey sources in various parts of our country is very wide; like Guangdong and Fujian, there are oranges, lychees, longans, yellow peels, rapeseed and other flowers for collection. Yunnan has gallyl, Jiangsu and Zhejiang have rapeseed, purple cloud, black cypress, wormwood, orange, orange, tea, etc. Sichuan has rapeseed, oranges, wild flowers, and the north has locusts, jujubes, etc.

In the Jiangsu and Zhejiang areas, it is also suitable for mobile transfer breeding, which can be transported by civil ships or trains; rapeseed and purple cloud are collected in spring, black cypress is collected in summer, wormwood is collected in autumn, and loquat and camellia are collected in winter.

However, the beekeeping industry in our country is still very young; and it is only like scattered sand with no unity and no organization. If everyone can unite and organize a honey sales cooperative, then not only will the honey outlet be large, but the number of bee colonies raised will also increase. I hope that those who care about rural side businesses will pay attention to this.

*Shen Bao* Local Supplement - Automobile Weekly

Active American Truck Market

— Moore

The American truck market has been very active recently. All commercial vehicle and truck manufacturers are showing bright prospects. It is a rare good phenomenon in recent years. Taking the domestic retail market in the United States as an example, in the first half of 1936, 300,000 trucks have been sold. In 1929, there were only 263,192. Therefore, people in the truck industry expect that the number of trucks sold this year may reach 600,000. Everyone is optimistic about achieving this goal.

Recently, the truck business has been developing rapidly. Although the weather in January was very cold, sales were 43,000 vehicles. The number of deliveries in February reached 40,000 vehicles. From February onwards, the sales curve gradually rose. By April, its record broke recent simultaneous records. The number of trucks sold reached 65,000, and the total sales in May were 60,000. In addition to the good phenomena in the domestic market, the number of trucks purchased by government agencies and various departments is also very large. Moreover, the number of exports is not included. Truck sales have shown a balanced development throughout the year. Almost every month of the year, all aspects are in urgent need of shares. The signs are very stable. Its signs are exactly the same as those hoped for by passenger car manufacturers. In the first six months of 1935, 50% of the truck industry was completed during this period. The business in the second half of the year did not exceed the first half. In 1934, 52% of the truck business was completed in the second six months. In a word, the truck industry has reached a very gratifying point. That is, buyers have changed their purchasing attitudes due to seasonal factors.

Most of the American truck industry this year comes from rural areas. The percentage is greater than any other aspect. American farmers own 26% of the total number of trucks in the country. In the worst days of the depression, they purchased only 8%. According to the estimates of the two major companies in this industry this year, the number of trucks purchased by rural areas can reach 30% of the total sales.

Because orders for trucks are increasing day by day, the assembly work of each car factory has also been restored accordingly. The stimulus in this regard is of course partly due to direct and indirect government funding. The number of trucks purchased by transportation companies is quite large. Especially in the companies that combine tractors and trailers. The number of new additions to large-scale motorcades is even greater. Several department stores are planning a new type of truck. Its load capacity is much greater than the now common trucks. Its capacity per square foot has increased a lot. Moreover, loading and unloading are much easier than before. The market sales of this type of car are obviously very broad. Because they have extraordinary advantages in daily use. Small businessmen, especially many shops in the suburbs, order the most of this type of car.

Various companies have implemented a 6% subsidy plan for customers who purchase trucks and passenger cars. This has indeed increased business a lot. The sales of large trucks are still continuing to increase. However, in order to reduce the taxes paid, small trucks sell better than large trucks. This year, because of the heavy licensing fees for one-and-a-half-ton vehicles, half-ton small vehicles are likely to rise and replace them. Recently, various car companies, in view of the popularity of small cars, have produced three-quarter-ton cars for the market. The "cab on the engine" type of truck has seen a large increase in sales due to its increased loading capacity, length not exceeding regulations, and increased operational efficiency. This phenomenon is not only the case for heavy-duty vehicles, but also for towing tractors and other vehicles.

Truck manufacturers have not ignored the appeal of streamlining. It is true that streamlining is attracting attention. However, the only element of a truck is its purpose. It must be consistent inside and out to complement each other. The trucks used by oil companies to transport oil products are all streamlined. When they are transported from the distribution station to the service station of the distributors, they swagger through the streets, which is also an excellent advertisement. Diesel engine vehicles will be popular in the future. However, they cannot compete in the market now. At present, a retail customer can buy a truck that runs entirely on gasoline for less money. If it is a diesel engine, the price will be much higher. The chassis, body, and other aspects are not included. However, at present, various well-known truck manufacturers are working hard to develop a good diesel engine vehicle. They must achieve the advantages of economy and ease of use. However, the selling price must be low in order to popularize it.

A Bunch of Automobile Briefs

— Yu

General Motors adds factory buildings The American General Motors Corporation has decided to build an eleven-story building to expand its research and experiment plant in Detroit. The cost is US$1,000,000. It is reported that this project has already begun. According to General Motors Vice President Knudson, this huge building is being built next to the existing factory building. The purpose of its construction is to implement General Motors' expansion plan. The lower seven floors of the new factory building will be occupied by the mechanical tool design department of the Fisher Body Plant. The upper four floors will be used by the General Motors Beauty Department. After the Fisher plant moves out of the main building, the empty building at its original site will be moved into by the Chevrolet Machinery Department. It is said that this new building will be completed in the fall of this year.

Sales of all vehicles have increased (1) In the first ten days of June this year, Studebaker's retail sales in the United States were 2,293 vehicles. The number for the same period in May was 2,179 vehicles. Passenger cars and trucks shipped from the factory, including exports, totaled 2,190 vehicles during this period. The number for the same period last year was only 999 vehicles. (2) In the four months from January to April of this year, the number of Chevrolet cars registered in the United States was 313,311. The number of registrations for its closest competitor was 247,981. In April, Chevrolet's registrations totaled 109,216 passenger cars and 22,633 trucks. Its closest competitor was (passenger cars) 84,239 and (trucks) 17,978. According to General Motors statistics, the registration ratio this year is 44.6% for passenger cars and 38.9% for trucks. (3) Nash and Lafayette cars increased by 92.6% in new car registration statistics in ten states, including New York, in the first three months of this year compared to a year ago. It is also reported that Nash Company exported a total of 16,637 Nash and Lafayette cars in the second quarter of its fiscal year, namely the three months of March, April, and May of this year. This is one of the company's largest export quarters in the past five years.

This local automobile registration statistics In the recent automobile registration in this city, Ford ranks first among the top ten. Automobile category: 1. Ford 5,152 vehicles; 2. Morris 962; 3. Austin 960; 4. Chevrolet 940; 5. Buick 730; 6. Vauxhall, including Barrila 510; 7. Plymouth 499; 8. Studebaker, including Logan 492; 9. Dodge 389; 10. Essex Water, including Toura car 357 vehicles. Truck category: 1. Ford 814 vehicles; 2. Chevrolet 273 vehicles; 3. Stewart 247; 4. Fentrell 222; 5. Studebaker 200; 6. Lever 177; 7. Great Monton-76; 8G.M.C 159; 9. Sterling Stevens 139; 10. Morris 108.

The Pagoda car factory plans to expand The Pagoda car factory is now working hard to expand. According to the factory's general manager, Mr. Klingiu, new machines have already been installed in the axle factory. This is the largest part of the entire 6,000,000 yuan expansion plan. In a few months, the newly installed machines will be able to be used. At that time, 850 workers will be added to adapt to the realization of the expansion plan.

Trucks make the most noise The Noise Reduction Committee of the 1st Avenue Association in New York is recently studying the sources of various noises on the road and trying to reduce them. According to the results of the research by the committee chairman, Mr. Price, the noises made by trucks are the loudest. The report given by the committee to its members is as follows: The air freight trucks of the Department of Health travel on the granite-paved road on First Avenue. The noise they make is the loudest and most annoying. The Committee has discussed prevention methods with Automobile Commissioner Hanai Tuomin. It is proposed to prohibit trucks from using solid tire wheels and chain drives for a period of two years.

Average towage of 110 miles The average towage mileage of American commercial trucks is 110 miles, according to a report by the Truck Committee of the American Automobile Manufacturers Association. According to the committee's report, this number was obtained from an investigation by the Federal Transportation Standards Council. The cargoes carried by trucks range from short-distance loads of sand and soil, etc., of 15 miles to long distances of 350 miles. The cargoes transported over long distances are mostly fresh fruits and vegetables that cannot be stored for a long time, which are more valuable and lighter in weight.

New Overseas Car Race News (Continued)

— Yun

Four-Cylinder Cars Again Dominate

May 30th is American Memorial Day. The Indianapolis auto race was held on this day. The champion was Mr. Mayhew from California. He drove a four-cylinder car. The average speed per hour was 109.069 miles. Mayhew is a three-time winning race car driver. This time, he broke his previous personal record with a four-cylinder car, which is also noteworthy. He had previously participated in the race with a compound cylinder car. In 1930, he drove a sixteen-cylinder car and finished fourth with a speed of 95.253 miles per hour. Among the cars participating this time, seven of the top ten were four-cylinder cars, three were eight-cylinder cars, and none were six-cylinder cars. Since 1911, ten victories have belonged to four-cylinder cars, and in 1934, 1935, and 1936, four-cylinder cars won the championship for three consecutive years. The entire Indianapolis race is 500 miles. The gasoline limit is 37 and a half gallons per car. When Mayhew finished the race, there were still three and a half gallons of gasoline left in the tank. On average, each gallon of gasoline can travel fifteen miles. Ten cars participating in the race were forced to withdraw before the finish line due to running out of gas. David Whalest, the general manager of the Whalest Wo Fuland Company, regarding the success of four-cylinder cars in the Indianapolis race, said that Mayhew's record proves that the speed and fuel economy of four-cylinder cars are undoubtedly achievable. According to Whalest, the car factory has 28 years of experience in manufacturing four-cylinder cars. Whalest also said that when Whalest cars can travel 35 miles per gallon of gasoline, the fuel consumption of other cars will be like Mayhew's car traveling a hundred miles per hour. In addition to fuel economy, the characteristics of four-cylinder cars also include excellent durability, as required in the 500-mile Indianapolis race. Therefore, it is said that the Whalest Company will continue to manufacture four-cylinder cars based on its 38 years of manufacturing experience.

New Seven-Mile Racetrack

The British are currently building a seven-mile auto racing track near Kirk City. If this plan can be realized according to budget, the highest speed auto races will be held on this new racetrack during the International Auto Race Festival. This planned racetrack includes a three-mile-long famous track between Kirk and Garri Lohan. British machine-powered cyclist, Mr. La Aite, set a world speed record of over 150 miles per hour several years ago. London racer, Fan Shousidun Haofu, recently drove a car in the Kirk Race. Afterwards, he said that he would like to hold a car race there in the next session. Fan said that this and an ideal track, the speed per hour should be between ninety and one hundred miles. Recently, several Irish auto racers also went to the site for inspection. The citizens of Kirk and auto racing enthusiasts all hope that the racetrack can be completed as scheduled. Mayor Frank has been elected as the chairman of the design committee. It is expected that this racetrack will be used for public competitions, with a prize of one thousand pounds. In the future, there will be no shortage of auto racers from Europe and Britain participating.

Harvard University Experiment: The Issue of Men and Women Driving Cars

— Yingdai

Proof that Men are Superior to Women

Regarding men and women driving cars, some people say that women are more careful than men, so their skills are particularly excellent and it is more difficult to cause accidents, and their driving skills are improving. Both sides hold their own opinions, and it is difficult to reach a consensus. But this time, Dr. Xueerhua of the Transportation Problem Research Association of Harvard University in the United States has conducted a practical test on men and women driving cars from the perspective of gender psychology and technology. According to him, there are currently no ideal car drivers of any age. In fact, women's driving skills are generally not as good as men's. At the same time, the research association also acknowledges that there are many reasons in humans themselves that can cause car accidents, and the only way to reduce such accidents is to start from education.

Dr. Xueerhua told us that women's physical skills and psychological inspiration in driving cars are not as good as men's, and they are not as easy to teach as men. Although it is very convenient to teach women over 20 years old to drive a car, it may be difficult for those between 25 and 30 years old to learn. As for men, among people of different ages, people around 23 years old are the most agile in encountering danger and traffic jams. Such people can immediately stop the vehicle in 41/100 of a second when they suddenly see danger ahead. In other words, at a speed of one mile per minute, he can stop the car at a distance of 35 feet. The action of stopping the car will gradually slow down with age for people over 23 years old. On the other hand, it is also known that children aged 15 to 16 have very slow stopping actions, similar to those aged 35 to 40. Harvard University's road experts are not limited to ordinary car roads in this experiment on the advantages and disadvantages of men and women driving cars. Because at the beginning of the experiment, drivers rarely encountered danger after driving for a long time on city roads. Therefore, Dr. Xueerhua adopted various experimental tools and placed them on the road to make drivers immediately encounter various simulated dangers. The most important experiment is to enable the driver to simultaneously handle the steering wheel, stop the car, distributor, and accelerator in a split second. With this skill, a driver will not encounter any danger on the road when driving out.

This experiment on stopping the car also paid special attention to proving the effectiveness of the fastest method in a few tenths of a second. From stepping on the accelerator to discovering the red light and immediately stopping the car. Unexpectedly, it is said that the experimental results show that a person who has drunk a small amount of alcohol is more agile in stopping the car than an ordinary person. This is certainly unexpected to us. Although other skills will decline after drinking alcohol, only stopping the car is improved. Among 4,000 drivers, the average stopping time was 41/100 of a second. At a speed of 60 miles per hour, ordinary drivers can stop the vehicle within 40 feet. The highest stopping record was 24/100 of a second. In fact, most people usually react more slowly when stopping the car, but it is particularly fast because of the experimental nature. In the end, the agility of stopping the car depends half on experience and half on talent.

Regarding women driving cars, there were also many who participated in this test. According to Dr. Xueerhua, women lack regularity when driving cars compared to men. However, the longer women drive, the more opportunities they have to improve, while men are like that from beginning to end, and there is no progress in the middle. The period of progress in men's driving skills lasts as long as ten years. From then on, it will decline. After about 25 years of experience, the driving skills of men and women can be said to be equal. If age and driving skills are matched, then those under 15 years old have very poor skills, and progress is fast after 15 years old, and even faster between 17 and 20 years old. It starts to decline from the age of 55. Facts tell us that after reaching this age, you should be extra careful when driving a car. As for this experiment, standard cars were used, and the roads passed were also very narrow.
